**Chapter One.**
**GENERAL PROVISIONS**

**Art. 1.** This Act shall regulate the ownership and management of waters on the territory of the Republic of Bulgaria as a national indivisible natural resource, and the ownership of water management systems and facilities.

**Art. 2.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The purpose of the Act is to ensure integrated water management in the interest of society and for the protection of public health, as well as to create conditions for:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) ensuring a sufficient quantity and good quality of surface and groundwater for

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 2 of 236

sustainable, balanced and equitable water use;
2. reducing water pollution;
3. protection of surface and groundwater and the waters of the Black Sea;
4. cessation of pollution of the marine environment with natural or synthetic substances;
5. reduction of discharges, emissions and losses of priority substances;
6. cessation of discharges, emissions and losses of priority hazardous substances;
7. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) prevention or reduction of the adverse consequences for human life and health, the environment, cultural heritage and economic activity, related to the adverse effects of waters.
(2) The objectives under para. 1 shall be achieved through:
1. prevention of deterioration, as well as protection and improvement of the status of aquatic ecosystems, of terrestrial ecosystems and wetlands directly dependent on them;
2. promotion of sustainable water use through long-term protection of available water resources;
3. complex, multiple and effective use of water resources;
4. application of measures for the protection and improvement of the aquatic environment;
5. ensuring a continuous reduction of groundwater pollution and preventing its pollution;
6. reduction of the consequences of floods and droughts;
7. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) flood risk assessment and management;
8. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015) carrying out control over the technical condition and safe operation of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities.

**Art. 2a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The objective under Art. 2 is achieved in compliance with the following principles:
1. recognition of waters as a vital resource and a common heritage, which is protected and safeguarded;
2. (suppl. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) determining the right of every citizen to access water for drinking and domestic purposes as a basic vital need is a priority of state policy and of the policy implemented by local self-government bodies;
3. defining river basins as the basic unit for integrated water management;
4. coordinating actions to achieve good water status in transboundary river basins at basin and national level and planning measures on the basis of equality and reciprocity in protecting national interests;
5. applying scientific and technical achievements in water management;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 3 of 236

6. applying economic regulators to achieve sustainable water use and protection;
7. preventing or reducing the adverse impact of waters, as well as restoring the damages;
8. preventing or reducing water pollution at the source of pollution;
9. maintaining and restoring vegetation and soil cover related to water reproduction;
10. the polluter pays the costs for measures to prevent, limit and reduce pollution, as well as to restore the damages;
11. cost recovery for water services;
12. cost recovery for water services, including the costs of the resource and environmental protection;
13. providing the public with timely, accurate and comprehensible information on the state of the waters, the planned measures and the results achieved from their implementation;
14. linking water protection activities with their sustainable use.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The management of activities related to the study, protection and management of waters, the operation and management of water management systems, shall be carried out by persons with a higher education degree of "Master" in the respective specialities.

**Art. 3.** Waters on the territory of the country are:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) surface waters;
2. groundwaters, including mineral waters;
3. internal sea waters and the territorial sea;
4. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) the waters of the Danube River, the Rezovska River and the Timok River within the state border of the Republic of Bulgaria.

**Art. 3a.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The fresh waters on the territory of the Republic of Bulgaria are national strategic resources.
(2) The sources of the waters under para. 1 are:
1. precipitation on the territory of the country;
2. inflow of transboundary waters from neighbouring countries, including half of the runoff of these waters, if they mark the state border and if not otherwise provided for in international treaties to which the Republic of Bulgaria is a party.
(3) The resources under para. 1 shall be managed in accordance with the procedure of this Act and taking into account the global change of the runoff-forming climatic factors in the region.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 4 of 236

**Art. 4.** (Rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)

**Art. 5.** The use of waters is carried out through water management systems, which include facilities for abstraction, storage, transportation, distribution, discharge and purification of waters, for the use of water energy and for protection from the harmful effects of waters.

**Art. 6.** The waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities on the territory of the country may be owned by the state, the municipalities, by natural and legal persons.

**Art. 7.** The regulation of relations concerning the ownership of waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities shall be based on the following principles:
1. the public significance of water as a valuable natural resource;
2. multi-purpose use of waters and water bodies to satisfy economic interests without prejudice to public interests and existing rights;
3. protection of the right of ownership over waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities, insofar as its exercise does not impair the integrity and unity of the hydrological cycle and the natural water system;
4. exercising the right of ownership in a way that does not violate the technological unity of the water management system.

**Art. 8.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) General water abstraction and use of water bodies and water abstraction for satisfying one's own needs is free of charge.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) For water abstraction and use of water bodies for the purpose of economic activity, a fee shall be paid for the use of the natural resource as a guarantee for creating equal legal conditions for economic activity for all citizens and legal entities.
(3) Persons carrying out the activities under paras. 1 and 2 are obliged to protect the environment.

**Art. 9.** (1) The waters under Art. 3 are managed at a national and basin level.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Water management at the national level is carried out by the Minister of Environment and Water.
(3) To assist the activity under para. 2, a Supreme Consultative Council on Water is established at the Ministry of Environment

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 5 of 236

and Water.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 108 of 2001, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 36 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 82 of 2009, in force from 16.10.2009, amend. - SG, No. 93 of 2009, in force from 25.12.2009, amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014, amend. - SG, No. 14 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2017, in force from 18.07.2017) The Supreme Consultative Council on Water includes representatives of the Ministry of Environment and Water, the Ministry of Regional Development and Public Works, the Ministry of Agriculture, Food and Forestry, the Ministry of Economy, the Ministry of Energy and the Ministry of Tourism, the Ministry of Transport, Information Technology and Communications, the Ministry of Health, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Interior, the Bulgarian Academy of Sciences, the municipalities, non-profit legal entities having a direct relation to waters, and others.
(5) The Minister of Environment and Water shall issue a Rulebook on the structure and activity of the Supreme Consultative Council on Water.
(6) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) Management at the basin level within one or several catchment areas is carried out in accordance with the state policy on waters by basin directorates for water management.

**Art. 10.** (1) The state policy related to the activities of operation, construction, reconstruction and modernization of water management systems and facilities is carried out by:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works - for water supply and sewerage systems and facilities in populated areas and for protection against the harmful effects of waters within the boundaries of populated areas;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 36 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 19 of 2011, in force from 09.04.2011, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2017, in force from 18.07.2017) the Minister of Agriculture, Food and Forestry:
a) for hydro-melioration systems and facilities and for protection from the harmful effects of waters outside the boundaries of populated areas;
b) through the Executive Agency for Forestry - for plantations in the systems and facilities under letter "a";
3. (amend. - SG, No. 108 of 2001, amend. - SG, No. 36 of 2006, in force from 01.07.2006, amend. - SG, No. 82 of 2009, in force from 16.10.2009, amend. - SG, No. 14 of 2015) the Minister of Energy - for hydro-energy systems and sites;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) the Minister of Environment and Water - for water abstraction facilities for mineral waters, public state property.

(2) The policy related to the activities of operation, construction, reconstruction and modernization of water management systems and facilities - municipal property, is carried out by the mayor of the municipality.
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) When implementing the policy under paras. 1 and 2, priority is given to the implementation of the measure programs included in the river basin management plans and in the flood risk management plans.
(4) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The policy related to the control over the technical condition and safe operation of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities is carried out by the chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance.

**Art. 10a.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) (1) The Council of Ministers shall determine the state policy for the Water Supply and Sewerage (WSS) sector as part of the country's water management policy and the National Strategy for Management and Development of the Water Sector in the Republic of Bulgaria.
(2) The Council of Ministers shall adopt a Strategy for the Development and Management of Water Supply and Sewerage in the Republic of Bulgaria for a period of not less than 10 years.
(3) The strategy under para. 2 shall determine the main goals, priorities, stages and necessary funds and sources of financing for the construction and development of WSS systems and for improving the quality of WSS services.
(4) The policy in the Water Supply and Sewerage sector is implemented by:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works;
2. municipal councils and mayors of municipalities.

**Art. 10b.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) The Minister of Regional Development and Public Works implements the state policy in the Water Supply and Sewerage sector at the national level by:

4. issuing subordinate normative acts related to the management and development of water supply and sewerage, in cases where this is provided for by law;

**Chapter Two.**
**RIGHT OF OWNERSHIP OVER WATERS, WATER BODIES AND WATER MANAGEMENT SYSTEMS AND FACILITIES**

**Section I.**
**State ownership of waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities**

**Art. 11.** The following waters and water bodies are public state property:
1. (suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the waters of the rivers and their appurtenant lands, as well as the waters in reservoirs, including those in dams - state property;
2. natural lakes, lagoons, limans, swamps and marshlands, when located on land - state property;
3. groundwaters, with the exception of mineral waters, regardless of whether they are located under state, municipal or private property;
4. natural waterfalls and their adjacent strips depending on the natural landscape, but not narrower than 10 m on both sides of the waterfall;
5. waters, including wastewaters, which flow from properties, public or private property, and flow into waters - public state property.

**Art. 12.** (1) Public state property are the islands and lands formed as a result of natural processes that have occurred in rivers, water bodies and islands in the internal sea waters and the territorial sea.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 11 of 236

(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Public state property are the seabed and its subsoil within the boundaries of the internal sea waters and the territorial sea and the coastal floodplain strip of the Danube River.

**Art. 13.** (Amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) (1) Public state property are the following water management systems and facilities:
1. the complex and significant dams according to Appendix No. 1, including their reservoirs up to the highest water level, their appurtenant facilities and their collecting diversions;
2. the facilities and devices - real estate, for measuring the quantity and quality of waters - public state property;
3. the systems and facilities for protection against the harmful effects of waters, built with state funds - protective dikes, river corrections and drainage systems, with the exception of those under Art. 19, para. 1, item 4, letter "d";
4. (amend. - SG, No. 95 of 2009) water abstraction facilities for mineral waters - exclusive state property, as well as observation boreholes, built with state funds;
5. water supply systems or parts thereof, through which water is supplied to the street water supply networks for consumers on the territory of more than one municipality;
6. treatment plants or facilities and facilities for disinfection of water for drinking and domestic purposes and public needs, for production, industrial and other activities of a commercial nature, when they are intended for consumers in more than one municipality;
7. the discharging sewerage collectors with their appurtenant facilities and the treatment plants and facilities for wastewater, which serve the consumers on the territory of more than one municipality.
(2) (Rep. - SG, No. 58 of 2015, new - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) Public state property are also the dams transferred free of charge by the municipalities to the state under the procedure of this Act.

**Art. 14.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Exclusive state property are:
1. internal sea waters and the territorial sea;
2. mineral waters according to the list in Appendix No. 2, which is an integral part of this Act.

**Art. 15.** (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Public state property are also the lands occupied by belt I of the sanitary-protection zones of the water sources and facilities for drinking and domestic water supply, public state property, and

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 12 of 236

of the water abstraction facilities for mineral waters under Art. 14, item 2.

**Art. 15a.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) Private state property are the building water supply installations and internal water supply networks and facilities, located in properties - state property, up to the measuring devices of the water supply connections for connection to the street water supply network and the sewerage networks and facilities discharging wastewater from these properties to the inspection shafts for connection to the street sewerage networks.

**Art. 16.** (1) State property over waters, declared public by this Act, may not be declared private state property.
(2) Outside the property declared as public state property by this Act, the state may own or acquire the right of ownership over waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities, which the law provides may be the subject of private ownership.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2015) The owners of agricultural land and forests, on which dams and water management facilities have been built, which have not been compensated for this in the respective order, shall be compensated in accordance with the procedure of Art. 10b and Art. 35 of the Act on Ownership and Use of Agricultural Land and of the Act on Restoration of Ownership of Forests and Lands from the Forest Fund.

**Art. 17.** (1) The waters, water bodies and water management facilities - state property, shall be documented in accordance with the requirements of the State Property Act.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Mineral waters shall be documented at the request of the Minister of Environment and Water on the basis of information provided by him.
(3) Copies of the deeds for the waters, water bodies and water management facilities, drawn up in the prescribed manner, shall be sent to the Ministry of Environment and Water within two months of the drawing up of the deeds.
(4) Paragraph 3 shall also apply when corrections are made to the deeds for state property.
(5) With regard to waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities - state property, the State Property Act shall apply, insofar as this Act does not provide otherwise.

**Art. 17a.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 96 of 2017, in force from 02.01.2018, suppl. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) Water abstraction facilities for mineral waters

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 13 of 236

under Art. 13, para. 1, item 4 may be built by the state, municipalities, when they have been granted management of mineral waters, exclusive state property, as well as by and for the account of persons who have been granted the right of water abstraction from mineral waters, through a new facility under the procedure of this law or a concession for the extraction of mineral water.
(2) The water abstraction facilities under para. 1 become the property of the state from the date of their commissioning.
(3) The persons under para. 1:
1. shall provide the Minister of Environment and Water with the documentation related to the construction of the facilities and the studies of the mineral water carried out in the process of building the facility, as well as all other data necessary for the inclusion of the facility in the public register of facilities for mineral waters under Art. 118d;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) shall transfer the facilities free of charge to the Minister of Environment and Water or to an official authorized by him, who shall take action before the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works to include the facility in the act for exclusive state property of the mineral water from the respective deposit;
3. shall manage the facility for the entire period for which the right of water abstraction has been granted;
4. shall provide the technical possibility for water abstraction from the facility and from other persons to whom the competent authority has granted such a right;
5. after the termination of the granted right of water abstraction or the concession for the extraction of mineral water, shall transfer the facility to the director of the respective basin directorate for management.

**Section II.**
**Municipal ownership of waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities**

**Art. 18.** (1) The ownership of the municipality over waters, water bodies, water management systems and facilities is public and private municipal property.
(2) Public municipal property over waters may not be declared private municipal property.

**Art. 19.** (1) (Previous text of Art. 19 - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) Public municipal property are:
1. waters and water bodies, including natural springs, lakes and swamps, when they are located on land - municipal property, and are not waters and water bodies under

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 14 of 236

Art. 11;
2. waters, including wastewaters, which flow from properties, public or private property, and flow into waters - public municipal property;
3. mineral waters, except those under Art. 14, item 2;
4. (suppl. - SG, No. 34 of 2001, suppl. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) water management systems and facilities on the territory of the municipality with the exception of those which are included in the property of commercial companies other than WSS operators with state and/or municipal participation in the capital or of irrigation associations and which are built with funds or with credits of the commercial companies or of the irrigation associations:
a) (amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) water supply systems or parts thereof, including networks and facilities for abstraction, purification, disinfection, storage and transportation of water, through which water is supplied to consumers on the territory of the municipality, with the exception of those under Art. 13, para. 1, items 5 and 6, as well as the street distribution water supply networks in urbanized territories and the water supply connections to the measuring devices in the properties of consumers;
b) (amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) street sewerage networks and storm water inlets in urbanized territories and the discharging sewerage collectors with their appurtenant facilities and the treatment plants and facilities for wastewater, which serve the consumers on the territory of the municipality, with the exception of those under Art. 13, para. 1, item 7;
c) (suppl. - SG, No. 34 of 2001, amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) dams, including those in the process of being built, with the exception of those under Art. 13, para. 1, item 1 and included in the property of commercial companies other than WSS operators with state and/or municipal participation, as well as their reservoirs up to the highest water level, and also their appurtenant facilities and collecting diversions;
d) protective dikes and facilities and systems for strengthening riverbeds within the boundaries of populated areas;
e) water transmission and water distribution networks for mineral waters;
f) (rep. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009)
5. (new - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009, amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) lands from belt I of the sanitary-protection zones of the water abstraction facilities and facilities for water supply of the populated areas in the municipality, with the exception of those under Art. 15 and Art. 24, item 11.
(2) (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009, rep. - SG, No. 58 of 2015, new - SG, No. 55 of 2018) Public municipal property, if they are not public state property, are also the real estate and the dams and their appurtenant facilities built on them, whose owners have waived their right of ownership in accordance with the procedure of Art. 100 of the Property Act.

Page 15 of 236

**Art. 19a.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) (1) The right of ownership over a dam - public municipal property, may be transferred free of charge to the state under the conditions and procedure of this Act after a decision of the municipal council.
(2) The right of ownership over a dam - public municipal property, granted under a concession, shall not be transferred.
(3) The decision under para. 1 is adopted by the municipal council upon a reasoned proposal by the mayor of the municipality. On the basis of the decision of the municipal council, the mayor of the municipality submits to the regional governor a reasoned proposal for the change of ownership of the dam. The decision of the municipal council and the act of municipal ownership for the dam, which is the subject of the decision, are attached to the proposal. A copy of the documents is sent to the Minister of Economy.

**Art. 19b.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) (1) The regional governor shall rule by order on the acceptance or refusal of the donation within one month of receiving the decision of the municipal council with the documents attached to it and shall notify the mayor of the municipality, the executive director of the State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams" and the Minister of Economy.
(2) The transfer of ownership is carried out through a donation contract concluded between the mayor of the municipality, whose property the dam is, and the regional governor. The contract between the regional governor and the mayor of the municipality is concluded within 14 days of the notification under para. 1. A copy of the registered contract is provided to the executive director of the State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams".
(3) For a dam transferred free of charge to the state, the regional governor draws up an act for public state property with granted management rights to the State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams".
(4) After registration of the act, the regional governor provides copies in accordance with Art. 70, para. 1 of the State Property Act.
(5) The regional governor refuses by order to accept the donation and returns the proposal and the accompanying file to the respective municipality when:
1. the water body declared for transfer by the municipality is not a dam under ยง 1, para. 1, item 94 of the additional provisions, or
2. the proposal relates to a dam granted under a concession, or
3. there is no act of municipal ownership.
(6) The order under para. 5 is subject to appeal under the procedure of the Administrative Procedure Code within 14 days of notification to the interested persons.

**Section III.**
**Private ownership of waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities**

**Art. 23.** The owner of the land is also the owner of the waters and water bodies in the property, unless they are the property of the state or the municipality.

**Art. 24.** Private property are:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 81 of 2000) waters originating within the boundaries of the private real estate, with the exception of mineral waters, while they flow through it, unless they are captured or included in the water supply systems;
2. lakes which are not fed by or through which do not flow waters - public state or public municipal property;
3. rainwater collecting within the boundaries of the real estate and the facilities built for this purpose;
4. waters flowing from the water bodies under items 1, 2 and 3, up to the point of their confluence with waters - public state or public municipal property;
5. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) the lands occupied by the waters under items 1, 2, 3 and 4;
6. wells in the real estate;
7. facilities and systems for the use, discharge and purification of waters, serving the respective property, as well as facilities for preventing and eliminating the consequences of the harmful effects of waters;
8. (new - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) WSS systems or parts thereof, built with funds of the consumers - natural or legal persons, which serve only the properties of these consumers;
9. (new - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) building water supply installations and internal water supply networks, located in the properties of consumers, up to the measuring devices of the water supply connections;
10. (new - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) sewerage networks and facilities, discharging wastewater from the properties of consumers to the inspection sewerage manhole for connection to the street sewerage networks;
11. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the lands from belt I of the sanitary-protection

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 18 of 236

zones of the facilities for individual drinking and domestic water supply.

**Art. 25.** (Rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)

**Art. 26.** The possession, use and disposal of waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities - private property, shall be carried out according to the general provisions for property, insofar as this Act does not provide otherwise.

**Section IV.**
**Co-ownership of water bodies and water management systems and facilities**

**Art. 27.** The right of ownership over a water body, water management system or facility may also belong jointly to two or more persons, when these objects are located in a co-owned property. In this case, the co-ownership of the water body, water management system or facility follows the co-ownership of the land, unless otherwise established.

**Art. 28.** (1) When partitioning a co-owned property in which there is a water body, the separation of real parts of the water body is not allowed.
(2) When partitioning a co-owned property in which there is a water body, the co-owner who has the right to a larger share of the property has a preference in the allocation of the water body.
(3) The remaining co-owners shall receive the monetary equivalent of their shares within 14 days after the conclusion of the partition contract, respectively from the entry into force of the court decision for the partition.

**Art. 29.** For matters not regulated in this section, the respective provisions of the Property Act shall apply.

**Section V.**
**Acquisition of the right of ownership over water bodies, water management systems and facilities**

**Art. 30.** (1) The acquisition of the right of ownership over water bodies and water management systems and facilities is carried out through a legal transaction for the land in which they are located, or by inheritance.
(2) Acquisition by prescription of water bodies, water management

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 19 of 236

systems and facilities - public state and municipal property, is not allowed.

**Art. 31.** (1) When the waters of the river, as a result of natural processes, including natural disasters, form a new bed and abandon the old one, the newly occupied place becomes public state property, and the abandoned place remains public state property.
(2) In this case, the affected owner is obliged to notify the body under Art. 10, para. 1, item 1 or 2, which, within a 6-month period, on the basis of a technical and economic analysis, takes action to correct the occurred changes.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2002, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2015) In the event that the measures taken lead to the return of the river to its old bed, the affected land owner restores his right of ownership over the plot. If this is technically impossible or economically inexpedient, the affected landowners are compensated with equivalent land from the state or municipal land fund under the procedure of Art. 10b of the Act on Ownership and Use of Agricultural Land.

**Art. 32.** The owner of a private water body does not acquire ownership over the land that the water covers in its extraordinary overflows.

**Section VI.**
**Restrictions on the right of ownership**

**Art. 33.** (1) The exercise of the right of ownership may be restricted in the following cases:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) when carrying out exploration and extraction of groundwater and abstraction of spring waters in a property, private property;
2. when building new objects related to the use, protection or defense against the harmful effects of waters, as well as for the more expedient utilization of water resources;
3. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) within the boundaries of the sanitary-protection zones of the facilities for drinking and domestic water supply and for mineral waters.
(2) If the implementation of the measures under para. 1 permanently deprives the owner of the use of the entire property or part of it, it shall be expropriated compulsorily under the procedure of the State Property Act.
(3) (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, rep. - SG, No. 61 of 2010)

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 20 of 236

(4) (Previous para. 3 - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The orders of the competent authority, issued on the grounds specified in this section, may not be executed before the entry into force of the act ordering the expropriation of the affected property and before the payment of the determined compensation.

**Art. 34.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Exploration and extraction of groundwater and abstraction of spring waters in a property - private property, may be carried out after the issuance of a permit for the performance of the respective activity.
(2) The activities under para. 1 are carried out on the basis of a written contract with the owner, which specifies the conditions for carrying out the activity and the due compensation.
(3) The competent authority under the provisions of this section proposes a draft contract to the owner, which must contain data on:
1. the necessary exploratory and/or construction and assembly works;
2. the part of the property that will be available to the contractor for the exploration or construction;
3. the part of the property that will remain occupied by the built facilities after the completion of the exploration or construction;
4. the deadline for completion of the exploration or construction;
5. the necessary works for land reclamation after the exploration or construction;
6. the monetary compensation, if during the exploration or construction the owner is deprived of the opportunity to use his property, as well as the procedure for payment of the compensation;
7. the annual monetary compensation, if part of the property remains occupied by the built facilities after the completion of the exploration or construction; the monetary compensation under this point is suspended after the restoration of the property to its original state;
8. other conditions that would create a guarantee for the protection of the property and the peace of the owner.
(4) The affected owner may respond within one month of receiving the proposal.
(5) If the affected owner does not accept the proposal within the period under para. 4, the rules for restricting ownership and for compensation, provided for in this section, shall apply.

**Art. 35.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) When, in the absence of another possibility, it is necessary to abstract spring waters in a property which is not state or municipal property,

**Art. 36.** (1) For the purpose of carrying out exploration of groundwater in a property - private property, the Minister of Environment and Water issues an order, which mandatorily specifies the circumstances under Art. 34, para. 3.

**Art. 38.** (1) When it is necessary to build new facilities related to the protection or defense against the harmful effects of waters, as well as for the satisfaction of such state or municipal needs that cannot be satisfied in another way, the compulsory expropriation of private properties, parts thereof or existing water management facilities is allowed after prior and equivalent compensation.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 36 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2017, in force from 18.07.2017) In the cases under para. 1, the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works or the Minister of Agriculture, Food and Forestry, depending on their competence, shall make a request for the compulsory expropriation of the affected real estate under the procedure of the State Property Act.
(3) The grounds for compulsory expropriation are the approved water management plans containing technical and economic studies proving that the state or municipal need cannot be satisfied in any other way.

**Chapter Three.**
**USE OF WATERS AND WATER BODIES**

**Art. 39.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The use of waters and water bodies includes water abstraction and use of the water body.

**Art. 40.** (1) (Previous text of Art. 40 - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The use of waters and water bodies is:
1. general and individual, depending on whether the holders of the right are an unlimited number of persons or individually determined persons;
2. (suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) with a permit or with prior written notification to the competent authority and without a permit, depending on whether the law provides for the issuance of an individual administrative act as a prerequisite for the creation of the right of use, or the right of use arises by virtue of another legal fact;
3. (rep. - SG, No. 36 of 2006, in force from 01.07.2006)
(2) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) An individual right to use waters and water bodies, granted by an administrative act to an individually determined person, may not be transferred to third parties.

**Art. 41.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) General water abstraction and use of water bodies is the right of citizens to use waters and/or water bodies - public state or municipal property, for personal needs, recreation and water sports, watering of animals and bathing.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The conditions and procedure for the use under para. 1 of waters and water bodies are determined for public state property by the regional governor, and for public municipal property - by the municipal council, in accordance with the issued permits for water abstraction and use of water bodies and in a way that guarantees the protection of the life and health of the population and the environment.
(3) The regional governor - for public state property, and the mayor of the municipality - for public municipal property, are obliged to announce:

**Art. 42.** (Amend. - SG, No. 70 of 2004, in force from 01.01.2005, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The owner of a water body, the water in which is public property, as well as the owner of a private water body, is obliged to announce the restrictions for general water abstraction or use, respectively a prohibition on this, through publication or in another way. The restrictions and prohibitions may be imposed for technological and hygienic-epidemiological reasons.

**Art. 43.** (1) Individual use of waters and water bodies exists,

**Art. 45.** (Rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)

**Art. 46.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) A permit for the use of a water body is issued for:

of the conductivity of uncorrected riverbeds for the purpose of clearing shrubs, woody vegetation and waste in the zones under Art. 119a, para. 1, item 5.
(2) The construction of structures, engineering-construction facilities, buildings and others, where contact with groundwater is made or is possible, is carried out under the conditions and procedure of the Spatial Development Act in compliance with the requirements for the protection of groundwater under Chapter Eight.
(3) A permit under para. 1, item 3 is issued under the procedure of this Act, except in cases where the issuance of a complex permit is provided for under the procedure of the Environmental Protection Act.

2. endangering the defense and security of the country;
3. violation of the conditions of the river basin management plans;
4. negative impacts on the banks, on the facilities, on the water quality and on protected territories or from the waste of water.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Public interests are also violated in the production and distribution in the commercial network of bottled natural mineral waters, carbonated or other beverages, which include mineral water without the corresponding certificate, without a legal basis and not in the legally established order.

**Chapter Four.**
**PERMIT REGIME**

**Section I.**
**General provisions**

**Art. 50.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) A permit is issued for water abstraction and for the use of a water body.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) For the issuance of permits for water abstraction and for the use of a water body, fees are paid, determined by a tariff from the Council of Ministers.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) A permit for water abstraction and/or for the use of a water body is issued:
1. to legal entities and sole traders;
2. to natural persons only when the request is for:
a) (rep. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018)
b) discharge of wastewater under Art. 46, para. 1, item 3;
c) mineral waters - exclusive state property, which have been granted for management and use by municipalities;
d) (amend. - SG, No. 12 of 2015) agricultural purposes by a registered farmer.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) When permitting water abstractions, the following order of satisfying the requests is observed:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) for drinking and domestic purposes;
2. treatment and prophylaxis - only for mineral waters;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) for agricultural purposes;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) other purposes, including industrial purposes, recreation and hydro-energy.
(5) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The priorities under para. 4 are applied in compliance with the environmental protection requirements.
(6) (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The permit for water abstraction under Art. 44 and the permit for the use of a surface water body under Art. 46 are issued under the conditions and procedure of this Act and of the ordinances under Art. 135, para. 1, items 1a and 13.
(7) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) A permit for groundwater abstraction

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 33 of 236

for waters under Art. 44 and a permit for the use of a groundwater body under Art. 46, para. 1, items 5, 6 and 7 are issued for water abstraction or for the use of a groundwater body:
1. through new facilities;
2. through existing facilities.
(8) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) In the cases under para. 7, item 1, a single general permit is issued, containing also the conditions for the construction of the facilities.
(9) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) The rights under the permit issued under the procedure of para. 8 may be exercised after:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) issuance of a construction permit under the procedure of the Spatial Development Act - for the rights to use a water body;
2. (suppl. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) amendment of the permit regarding the parameters of the permitted water abstraction or use, which is carried out ex officio by the director of the basin directorate, depending on the results of the study of the groundwater in the process of construction of the facilities - for the rights to water abstraction.
(10) (New - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) The provisions of paras. 7 - 9 do not apply to deposits of mineral waters, exclusive state property, granted free of charge for management and use by municipalities. In these cases, the director of the basin directorate issues a separate permit for the use of a water body for the construction, repair or reconstruction of a facility for water abstraction of mineral water from the respective deposit.
(11) (New - SG, No. 12 of 2017, former para. 10 - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) When from the activity of the facility, which is planned to be supplied with water, wastewater containing priority substances within the meaning of the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 17 or hazardous substances within the meaning of the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 2 is formed, and the WSS operator of the consolidated territory certifies that it cannot include the wastewater in the sewerage system:
1. together with the application for a permit for water abstraction, an application for a permit for the discharge of wastewater into surface water bodies is also submitted;
2. the procedure for issuing a permit for water abstraction is carried out in coordination with the procedure for issuing a permit for the use of a surface water body for the discharge of wastewater.

**Art. 50a.** (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) (1) The permits under Art. 50, para. 1 are reviewed regarding compliance with the environmental protection objectives under Art. 156a, when:
1. data from monitoring or other information and assessments show that the environmental protection objectives established for a water body are not being met or there is a risk of deterioration of the status of a water body or the potential of an artificial or heavily modified water body;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 34 of 236

2. non-compliances have been found between the hydromorphological conditions and the ecological status of a water body or the good ecological potential of an artificial or heavily modified water body;
3. for the water body, exceptions under Art. 156b - 156g have been justified, requiring the fulfillment of certain conditions.
(2) The permits under Art. 50, para. 1 are reviewed with each update of the characterization of the river basin management district under Art. 156h.
(3) When the exercise of the rights under a permit under Art. 50, para. 1 represents a pressure on the state of the waters, contributing to the deterioration of the state or the failure to achieve the environmental protection objectives, or for the non-fulfillment of the conditions under Art. 156b - 156g, the director of the basin directorate plans an amendment of the permit, and when the objectives or conditions cannot be met with an amendment - its termination, notifying the holder of the permit and performing the actions under Art. 74, para. 1, item 1.
(4) The amendment or termination of the permit under Art. 50, para. 1 is included in the programs of measures in the respective river basin management plan.

**Art. 51.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) (1) For the protection of waters and the determination of conditions for this when coordinating the overall projects for prospecting and exploration under Art. 82, para. 1 of the Underground Resources Act, the Ministry of Environment and Water is provided with information on:
1. the location of the area in which the exploration of underground resources is planned;
2. the surface and groundwater bodies falling within the area under item 1, which may be affected by the planned activities, and how they will be affected;
3. the rock or lithological variety representing the underground resource;
4. the depth to which the exploration will be carried out.
(2) For the protection of waters and the determination of conditions for this when granting a concession for the extraction of underground resources, a plan for the development of the deposit is submitted for coordination, which, in addition to the information under para. 1, also contains the results of the completed exploration related to:
1. detailing the geological section;
2. the groundwater level in the area of the explored site.

**Art. 52.** (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The permit is issued by:
1. the Minister of Environment and Water or an official authorized by him for:

aa) the dams in Appendix No. 1, including for the discharge of wastewater;

**Art. 53.** (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The manner of using the waters of the complex and significant dams in Appendix No. 1 is determined in annual and monthly operational schedules, which are approved by the Minister of Environment and Water and are an integral part of the water abstraction permit.
(2) The annual schedule determines the strategy for using the waters of the dams in Appendix No. 1 during the respective year.
(3) The monthly schedule is prepared taking into account the current information on the state of the dam in the previous month, the strategy determined by the annual schedule, the forecast for the expected inflow, the hydro-meteorological situation and the assessment of the requests in the monthly application from the holders of

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 36 of 236

water abstraction permits.
(4) The monthly schedules shall:
1. transfer waters;
2. determine free volumes to accommodate expected inflow;
3. determine specific conditions for the permit holders.
(5) The permitted limit may be exceeded in the case of a volume determined by the monthly schedule for accommodating an expected inflow or in the event of unforeseen and/or exceptional circumstances.
(6) The persons who carry out the technical operation of the dams and their appurtenant facilities shall submit to the Ministry of Environment and Water daily, ten-day and monthly, on the next working day, information on the water management balance in the dams in Appendix No. 1.
(7) The Minister of Environment and Water or an official authorized by him, in the event of unforeseen and/or exceptional circumstances, shall amend the monthly schedule, for which he shall notify the interested parties in writing.

**Art. 54.** The construction of diversions for the transfer of water between river basins is carried out by a decision of the National Assembly.

**Art. 55.** When issuing a permit, the authorities under Art. 52, para. 1 shall take into account:
1. the available water resources;
2. the needs of the applicant for water user, respectively user of a water body;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the state of the water body, the environmental protection objectives set for the respective water body, and the measures to achieve these objectives, defined in the river basin management plans;
4. the acquired rights.

**Art. 56.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The permit for water abstraction under Art. 44 and the permit for the use of a water body under Art. 46 shall contain:

2. the number and date of issuance of the act;
3. the legal and factual grounds for issuing the act;

4. a deadline for achieving the individual emission limits;
5. quantities of discharged wastewater - maximum hourly, average daily and annual.
(5) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The conditions under which the permits are issued are determined by the ordinances under Art. 135, para. 1, items 1a and 2 and are formed as an appendix - an integral part of the permit.
(6) Schemes and/or maps on an appropriate scale may be attached to the permit, depending on the specifics of the permit for water abstraction or use of a water body.
(7) (Rep. - SG, No. 61 of 2010)

**Art. 57.** (1) The permit is issued for a period:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) up to 35 years - for impoundment of and for water abstraction from complex dams for hydro-energy and hydro-melioration purposes;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) up to 25 years - for water abstraction for drinking and domestic water supply;
2a. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, rep. - SG, No. 61 of 2010)
3. (amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) up to 20 years - in the other cases.
(2) (Rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) Permits for the use of a water body for the extraction of alluvial deposits are issued for a period not longer than the period of validity of the river basin management plan in force at the date of issuance of the permit. In the cases under Art. 140, the permit is issued to the person selected as the contractor for these activities, for the period of performance of the contract concluded between him and the regional governor.
(4) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Permits for the use of a water body for the discharge of wastewater under Art. 46, para. 1, item 3, letter "a" are issued for a period until the commissioning of the facility/sewerage system.

**Art. 58.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) A permit is not required, but only a 30-day prior written notification to the basin directorate is necessary for the performance of the following activities:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) development, modernization

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

or technological renewal of existing installations and technological processes for which a permit for water abstraction and/or use of a water body has been issued, where the impact permitted by the issued permit is not changed;

(amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) use of surface waters by means of temporary abstraction facilities necessary for the construction of a given construction site, when the abstracted water quantity is less than 10 liters per second and the resulting flow after use does not affect the quality of the water;
3. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010, suppl. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) aerial crossing of facilities over the water body;

**Art. 59.** (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The permit is issued on the basis of:

**Section II.**
**Conditions and procedure for issuing a permit**

**Art. 60.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) To open a procedure for the issuance of a permit, the applicants shall submit an application in a form approved by the Minister of Environment and Water, which shall state:
1. the data under Art. 56, para. 1, items 4 - 9;
2. a correspondence address, including an electronic address - if available;
3. a telephone and fax number for contact with the natural person or with the person who manages and represents the company under Art. 56, para. 1, item 4;
4. the parameters of the requested use;
5. the number of the decision of the Minister of Environment and Water or of the director of the respective regional inspectorate of environment and water on the environmental impact assessment or on the screening that an environmental impact assessment is not necessary, or on the assessment of compatibility, when such are required under the Environmental Protection Act and the Biological Diversity Act;
6. (new - SG, No. 13 of 2021) registration card number for farmers, where applicable.
(2) The following shall be attached to the application under para. 1:
1. (suppl. - SG, No. 13 of 2021) a certified document for a paid fee for issuing the permit, when the payment is not made electronically;
2. (suppl. - SG, No. 13 of 2021) an up-to-date sketch or map of the properties where the activity will be carried out, certified by the respective competent authority, or a reference with the individualizing data of the properties and the administrative issuing authority, on the basis of which information can be collected ex officio;

(3) When the request is for the issuance of a permit for water abstraction from surface waters, the application under para. 1 shall also be accompanied by:

b) the content of the attached documents under Art. 60 meets the requirements of this Act;

(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) When the requirements under Art. 60 are not met, the authority under para. 1 notifies the applicant to rectify the inconsistencies within a period of up to two months.
(4) (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, suppl. - SG, No. 13 of 2021) If the inconsistencies are not rectified within the period under para. 3, the documents are not reviewed and no procedure is opened, of which the applicant is notified in writing within three days.
(5) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) If, during the assessment under Art. 62, para. 1, carried out within the period under para. 2, it is established that the request does not meet the requirements of Art. 62, para. 1 and the conditions under Art. 68 are present, the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 issues a decision with a reasoned refusal to issue a permit. **Section III.**
**Amendment and extension of the permit**

**Art. 72.** (1) (Previous text of Art. 72, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) An amendment of the permit may be made:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) ex officio by the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 - under the conditions of Art. 73;
2. at the request of the person in whose favor it is granted.
(2) (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) In the cases under para. 1, item 2, the authority under para. 1 checks the fulfillment of the conditions of the issued permit.

**Art. 73.** (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) (1) The permits issued under this Act are amended ex officio by the authority under Art. 52, para. 1, when:
1. during the characterization of the river basin management district, in the process of developing the river basin management plans, it is established that

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 50 of 236

the respective water body cannot achieve the objectives under Art. 156a for good status or potential with the current pressure on the waters from the respective activities and it is necessary to fulfill the conditions under Art. 156b - 156g - for justification of exceptions;
2. for a water body for which an exception from the objectives under Art. 156a for achieving good status or potential has been justified in the previous river basin management plan and the new assessment shows that a further reduction of the pressure is necessary in order to fulfill the conditions under Art. 156b - 156g;
3. regardless of compliance with the conditions in the permit, contradictions with public interests arise.
(2) The permits under para. 1, items 1 and 2 are amended from the date of adoption of the respective river basin management plan.
(3) The permits under para. 1, item 3 are amended under the procedure of Art. 75 - 77.

**Art. 74.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) After establishing the circumstances:
1. under Art. 73, para. 1, items 1 and 2, the director of the basin directorate prescribes to the permit holders conditions and/or restrictions for the use of waters for the permitted purposes and notifies the respective authorities under Art. 52, para. 1 of the necessary amendments and their inclusion in the program of measures;
2. under Art. 73, para. 1, item 3, the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 starts an ex officio procedure for amendment of the permits to ensure compliance with public interests.
(2) The prescribed conditions or restrictions must meet the following requirements:
1. proportionality of the imposed restrictions and the expected benefits;
2. minimal interference with existing rights;
3. the restrictions shall be imposed by indicating their sequence in accordance with the changing water management relations.

**Art. 75.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 101 of 2015, in force from 22.12.2015, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) The amendment of the permit is announced under the procedure of Art. 62a, when the amendment is at the request of the person in whose favor it is granted or under the procedure of Art. 73, para. 1, item 3 and the parameters of the permitted use of water are changed.
(2) The announcement of the amendment of the permits under Art. 73, para. 1, items 1 and 2 is made with the announcement of the draft of the respective river basin management plan.

**Art. 76.** (1) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The authority under Art. 52, para. 1:

**Art. 77.** (1) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Until the issuance of a decision for amendment or for refusal to amend the permit, the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 reviews the objections of the person in whose favor it is issued, the requests and objections as a result of the announcement under Art. 75, submitted in writing.
(2) The review of the documents under para. 1 does not lead to a suspension of the period under Art. 76, para. 1.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 30 of 2006, in force from 12.07.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, suppl. - SG, No. 77 of 2018, in force from 01.01.2019) The decision for amendment or for refusal to amend the permit may be appealed before the respective administrative court under the procedure of the Administrative Procedure Code.

**Art. 78.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) An application for the extension of the validity of a permit is submitted before its expiration to the authority under Art. 52, para. 1.
(2) The authority under Art. 52, para. 1 extends the validity of the permit when:
1. the application is submitted within the period under para. 1;
2. normative provisions, planning provisions or public interests are not violated, and
3. the conditions of the issued permit have been met.
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The provisions of paras. 1 and 2 also apply when an amendment and extension of the validity of a permit is requested simultaneously.

**Section IV.**
**Termination of the validity of the permit**

**Art. 79.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The validity of the issued permit is terminated upon the expiration of its term or by a decision of the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 in case of:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) termination of the water user's right of ownership or use over the real estate where the activity is carried out or where the water abstraction facility is located, as well as in case of an explicit waiver of the right to use the respective water body;
2. (rep. - SG, No. 61 of 2010)
3. (suppl. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) death of the natural person, respectively termination of the legal entity or striking-off of the sole trader;
4. natural or artificial disappearance of the water body;
5. (rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)
6. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) permanent changes in the technical parameters of the water abstraction facility, making its use impossible;
7. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010, rep. - SG, No. 58 of 2015)
8. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the circumstances under Art. 50a, para. 3, as of the date of adoption of the river basin management plan.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) In the cases under para. 1, items 1 and 3, the persons who have acquired the rights of ownership or use of the real estate, respectively the successors of the persons under item 3, shall, within three months, notify in writing the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 whether they wish to use the rights under the issued permit.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) If the applicants meet the conditions for issuing a permit and the period under para. 2 is observed, the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 terminates the permit within a 20-day period and reissues the permit in their name.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) If the applicants do not meet the conditions for issuing a permit, the authority under Art. 52, para. 1 refuses to reissue the permit in their name. When the persons have used the right to use the waters within the period until receiving the decision, they shall pay the due fees for this under Art. 194.
(5) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) If the period under para. 2 is not observed, the permit is considered terminated from the date of the occurrence of the circumstances under para. 1 and a new permit is issued under the general procedure.

**Section V.**
**Restriction of rights arising from the permit**

**Art. 83.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The rights of water abstraction arising from the permit may be additionally restricted after the issuance of the permit.
(2) The restriction under para. 1 is allowed for the protection of the life and health of the population, the defense and security of the country and the cultural and historical heritage.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The restriction of water abstraction and/or use is imposed regardless of the procedure under Section III of this chapter.

**Art. 84.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The restriction of water abstraction is carried out by a decision of the authority that issued the permit.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The decision under para. 1 changes the limits for water abstraction for a certain period of time.
(3) The limits under para. 2 are the maximum permissible volumes for water abstraction, which are determined for one or more water users.
(4) The period of restriction may not exceed the duration of the causes imposing the restriction.

**Art. 85.** When determining the limits, the state of the water body, the priority of drinking and domestic water supply, the declared water needs and

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

the conditions in the respective permits are taken into account.

**Art. 86.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) In the event of circumstances that threaten the life and health of the population in certain regions of the country, the Council of Ministers may impose restrictions on the use of waters, affecting all water users in the region, as well as their subscribers, if any.

**Art. 87.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) In the cases under this section, the affected water users and their subscribers cannot seek liability from the state for the damages caused.
