**Chapter Seven.**
**LAND SERVITUDES RELATED TO WATER BODIES**

**Section I.**
**General provisions**

**Art. 103.** (1) A land servitude is a burden imposed on a real estate, called a servient estate, in favor of another real estate, called a dominant estate, which belongs to another owner.
(2) A land servitude arises from the law or from a legal transaction.
(3) A land servitude may be acquired by prescription through 10-year use.

**Art. 104.** (1) Servitudes established by law are for public or private use.
(2) (Suppl. - SG, No. 34 of 2001) Servitudes established for public use relate to ensuring access for general use of water bodies - public property, and to the construction of the necessary infrastructure for this, as well as for

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 59 of 236

maintenance of water management systems and facilities intended to provide the service of water supply for the population and for irrigation.

**Art. 105.** The legal land servitudes for private use are those that arise from the location of the lands and the right of passage and water conveyance.

**Art. 106.** When exercising servitudes, the following rules are observed:
1. a change of ownership of the property does not terminate the effect of the servitudes either with respect to the dominant or with respect to the servient estate;
2. if the owners of the servient estate are several persons, a servitude by legal transaction may be established only with the consent of all co-owners;
3. a granted servitude by legal transaction is binding on the successors of the owner of the servient estate;
4. the holder of the servitude is obliged, when carrying out the necessary actions for its exercise, to cause the least possible inconvenience to the owner of the servient estate and to bear the necessary expenses for this, unless otherwise agreed;
5. servitudes are indivisible rights; they can be exercised in full for the benefit of each part of the dominant estate and encumber in full each part of the servient estate, even if the properties are divided;
6. the servitude may be used only for the needs of the dominant estate;
7. the owner of the servient estate does not have the right to move the servitude;
8. servitudes established by legal transaction are extinguished:
a) in case of objective impossibility of their exercise;
b) upon the merger of the two properties as a result of a legal transaction;
c) after the expiration of the term of the contract;
d) after non-use for a period of 10 years.

**Art. 107.** (1) The local jurisdiction of disputes over the exercise of servitudes under this chapter is determined by the location of the dominant and servient estate.
(2) The compensations under this chapter are determined according to current market prices.

**Section II.**
**Servitudes arising from the location of the properties**

**Art. 108.** (1) The owners of the properties located upstream do not have the right to impede the natural runoff of waters and to aggravate the burdens borne in

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 60 of 236

connection with this restriction by the downstream properties.
(2) The owners of the downstream properties are obliged to accept the water that flows naturally from the upstream properties.

**Art. 109.** (1) If the banks or the facilities for retaining water in the dominant estate are in a condition that does not provide protection from the influence of the waters, its owner is obliged to carry out the necessary construction works so that the owner of the servient estate does not suffer any damage.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 81 of 2000) If the obligated owner does not carry out the necessary construction works, the owners of the servient estate, if they suffer damage or if they are in danger of suffering damage, may carry out the necessary works in the dominant estate at their own expense with the prior permission of the court after hearing the interested persons.
(3) The rule of para. 2 also applies when, in a property, as a result of the construction of a tailings pond, a slime pond or a dump, accumulations occur which change the flow of the waters, and as a result, the water causes or may cause damage to neighboring real estates.
(4) The owners who participated in the expenses for carrying out the necessary works for strengthening the banks, repairing the facilities or clearing the accumulations have the right to compensation for damages from the person who caused the destruction of the banks or facilities or the formation of the accumulations.

**Art. 110.** (1) The owner through whose real estate a watercourse passes may use it according to the requirements of the law, without also violating the right of the owner of the downstream real estate.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) In the case of para. 1, the owner of the downstream property may carry out works that affect the natural state of the water body, according to the conditions of the water abstraction permit and without causing damage to the owner of the upstream property.

**Art. 111.** The owner of a water body disposes of its waters without causing damage to neighboring real estates.

**Section III.**
**Right of water conveyance**

**Art. 112.** (1) Every owner is obliged to grant the right of water conveyance through his property to all who have a permanent or temporary need for it.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 61 of 236

(2) If the construction of pipelines or facilities for water conveyance is necessary, servitude strips with a size not greater than the diameter of the pipeline or the size of the facilities, increased by 60 cm, are determined, on which construction and planting of permanent crops are not permitted.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The right of water conveyance through another's property is established by an agreement between the owners of the dominant and servient estate, and if such an agreement cannot be reached - by an act of the authority under Art. 52, para. 1, item 4 in compliance with the procedure of Art. 34 and 36, without ordering expropriation of the affected property.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The exercise of the rights under the act of the authority under Art. 52, para. 1, item 4 is permissible only after payment of the determined compensation.

**Art. 113.** (1) The water conveyance through another's property is carried out in a manner corresponding to the relief, taking into account existing buildings and permanent crops.
(2) The owner of the dominant estate, in the case under para. 1, is obliged to pay the price of the land that will be occupied, increased by one-fifth, in addition to the direct damages and those that arise from the division of the land, if a surface flow is created. For the part of the land that will be occupied by the collection of the excavated earth masses, half of the price, increased by one-fifth, is paid.

**Art. 114.** Unless otherwise agreed, for the right of water conveyance, the following rules are observed:
1. the holder of the right of water conveyance is obliged, after the expiration of the period, to restore the original state of the respective property;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) if it is necessary to carry out new works or to change the quantity of the flowing water due to a change in the water abstraction permit, the changes regarding the burden on the servient estate may not be made before payment of the due amount for this;
3. the owner of the servient estate has the right to demand that the bed of the water be determined with the placement of permanent boundaries at the expense of the holder of the servitude; the latter is obliged to build the necessary facilities if the owner of the servient estate does not have free access to his property as a result of the water conveyance.

**Art. 115.** The owner through whose property foreign waters pass as a result of the exercise of a servitude may use them according to the requirements of the law, by bearing the corresponding part of the expenses for the construction and maintenance of the facilities, unless otherwise agreed.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 62 of 236

**Chapter Eight.**
**PROTECTION OF WATERS AND WATER BODIES**

**Art. 116.** (1) (Suppl. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) All waters and water bodies are protected from depletion, pollution and damage in order to maintain the necessary quantity and quality of waters and a healthy environment, preserve ecosystems, preserve the landscape and prevent economic losses, including:
1. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) achieving good chemical and ecological status of surface waters;
2. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) achieving good quantitative and chemical status of groundwaters;
3. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) reducing the need to treat waters before their use;
4. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) ensuring the development of aquatic ecosystems and related terrestrial ecosystems.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) To achieve the objectives under para. 1, the following are determined:
1. a minimum permissible flow in rivers;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) measures for the protection of the quantity and quality of waters, including waters intended for drinking and domestic water supply;
3. zones for water protection;
4. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the altitude of the permissible drawdown of the water level for each groundwater body or for part of a water body;
5. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) annually the natural and available resources of groundwater bodies based on current hydrological and hydrogeological data;
6. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) monthly the total abstraction from groundwater bodies and the free water volumes;
7. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the dynamic reserves of the solid runoff of rivers;
8. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) restrictions when issuing permits for:
a) (amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) use of the Danube River and reservoirs for the extraction of alluvial deposits;
b) water abstraction from surface waters for the production of electricity;
c) water abstraction from groundwaters.

**Art. 117.** (1) For the protection of aquatic ecosystems and wetlands, a minimum permissible flow in rivers is determined.
(2) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The flow under para. 1 is determined in the plans for

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 63 of 236

river basin management in accordance with the methodology under Art. 135, para. 1, item 1.
(3) For the purpose under para. 1, the following measures are applied:
1. limiting the degree of flow regulation;
2. determining mandatory water quantities to be released from dams;
3. introducing restrictions on the transfer of water from one river basin to another;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) introducing a ban on the issuance of new permits for water abstraction and restricting already issued permits;
5. carrying out afforestation measures.
(4) When developing water management balances, the minimum water quantities for flooding are provided with priority.

**Art. 117a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the protection of the quantity of waters and ensuring their effective use when providing water services, water consumption norms are determined.
(2) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014, amend. - SG, No. 14 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2017, in force from 18.07.2017) The water consumption norms under para. 1 are determined by an ordinance of the Council of Ministers upon a proposal from the Minister of Economy, the Minister of Energy, the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works, the Minister of Agriculture, Food and Forestry, the Minister of Health and the Minister of Environment and Water.

**Art. 118.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the purpose of protecting waters, the Minister of Environment and Water shall, by order, determine the priority and priority hazardous substances.
(2) Waters and water bodies are protected from pollution and damage by:
1. cessation of the introduction of priority hazardous substances into waters;
2. continuous reduction of the introduction of priority substances into waters;
3. restriction of the introduction of hazardous and other substances into waters;
4. construction of treatment plants for wastewater;
5. (new - SG, No. 44 of 2020, in force from 14.05.2020) the free movement of the necessary chemicals for the treatment of drinking and wastewater during the treatment processes, including import across the state border;
6. (former item 5 - SG, No. 44 of 2020, in force from 14.05.2020) establishing a regime of use and protection of coastal floodplains;
7. (former item 6 - SG, No. 44 of 2020, in force from 14.05.2020) regulating prohibitions on the disposal of waste and hazardous substances in places from where it may

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

cause water pollution;
8. (former item 7 - SG, No. 44 of 2020, in force from 14.05.2020) determining measures to prevent the artificial mixing of groundwaters of different qualities.
(3) (Rep. - SG, No. 61 of 2010)
(4) The Minister of Environment and Water and the Minister of Health shall determine the maximum permissible concentrations and emission norms for radionuclides in waters and water bodies.
(5) The order under para. 1 is promulgated in the "State Gazette".

**Art. 118a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the protection of groundwaters from pollution, the following are prohibited:
1. (In force from 22.12.2013) the direct discharge of pollutants into groundwaters, except in the cases under para. 2;
2. the disposal, including landfilling, of priority substances that may lead to the indirect discharge of pollutants into groundwaters;
3. other activities on the surface and in the groundwater body that may lead to the indirect discharge of priority substances into groundwaters;
4. the use of materials containing priority substances in the construction of structures, engineering-construction facilities and others, where contact with groundwater is made or is possible;
5. the mixing of groundwaters of different quality through the construction of water abstraction facilities;
6. the injection of natural gas or liquefied petroleum gas into groundwater bodies, except in the cases under paras. 3 and 4.
(2) Direct discharge of pollutants in small quantities into groundwaters is allowed in cases where this is for scientific purposes for characterization, protection and restoration of water bodies and these quantities are strictly limited to the size necessary for the respective purpose.
(3) Injection for the storage of natural gas or liquefied petroleum gas is allowed in parts of the earth's crust that are naturally permanently unsuitable for other purposes.
(4) Injection for the storage of natural gas or liquefied petroleum gas in parts of the earth's crust outside the cases under para. 3 is allowed when there is a priority need to ensure gas supply and in a manner that ensures the prevention of any future danger of deterioration of the quality of groundwaters.
(5) In the cases under para. 4, the injection is carried out after a hydrogeological study and an assessment of the risk of pollution of groundwaters, proving that the state of the groundwaters into which the injection is carried out will not deteriorate and there is no danger of deterioration of the state of other groundwaters in the injection area.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 65 of 236

(6) In the cases under paras. 2, 3 and 4, a permit is issued under the conditions and procedure of this Act.
(7) A permit for the injection and reinjection of waters is also issued in the cases of:
1. injection of waters containing substances resulting from the exploration and extraction of oil and gas or from mining activities;
2. injection of waters for reasons of a technical nature in parts of the earth's crust from which oil and gas or other substances have been extracted or for natural reasons are permanently unsuitable for other purposes.
(8) The injected waters under para. 7, item 1 may not contain substances other than those obtained as a result of the exploration and extraction of oil and gas or from mining activities.
(9) A permit for reinjection is also issued in the cases of:
1. dewatering of mines, quarries and engineering-construction facilities;
2. use of waters for the extraction of hydrogeothermal energy.
(10) A permit under paras. 2, 3, 4, 7 and 9 is not issued when, as a result of this activity, preconditions are created for not achieving the environmental protection objectives for the respective water body.

**Art. 118b.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) For the protection of groundwaters, a pollution threshold and a starting point for taking measures to reverse identified significant and sustained upward trends in the concentration of pollutants in groundwaters are determined.
(2) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The pollution threshold may be established at the national level or for each river basin management district or part of an international river basin management district or for a groundwater body or group of bodies.
(3) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The pollution threshold and the starting points under para. 1 at the basin level are determined in the river basin management plans.
(4) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The updating of the list of substances for which a pollution threshold and starting points under para. 3 are determined and their concentration is carried out with the updating of the river basin management plans.

**Art. 118c.** (1) (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, former text of Art. 118c - SG, No. 58 of 2015) Water abstraction from groundwaters is not permitted when:

body permissible drawdown;

**Art. 118g.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) Water abstraction from surface waters for the production of electricity is not permitted:
1. (suppl. - SG, No. 12 of 2017) in case of cascade construction of diversion and run-of-river type hydropower plants, unless they are of significant public interest and/or the benefits to society exceed the benefits of achieving the environmental objectives and are justified as an exception under Art. 156e in the current river basin management plan;

(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The use of the Danube River and reservoirs for the extraction of alluvial deposits is not permitted when the extraction creates a risk of violating the stability of existing hydrotechnical or other facilities.
(4) The use of a water body for the construction of new corrections is not permitted when this part of the river falls into protection zones under Art. 119a, para. 1, item 5, except for:
1. corrections in populated areas;
2. corrections aimed at restoring natural habitats and river meandering;
3. construction of bottom and hydraulic sills necessary for the restoration of the river level in corrected sections;
4. corrections through dredging and construction of facilities to ensure conditions for navigation, including for the protection of banks and islands in the Danube River;
5. when they are for protection against the harmful effects of waters.

**Art. 124.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the protection of waters from pollution, maximum permissible concentrations of substances in industrial wastewaters discharged into sewerage networks or into treatment plants for wastewater of populated areas and settlement formations are determined.
(2) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The maximum permissible concentrations under para. 1 are determined by the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 11.

**Art. 125.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Only wastewaters that can be treated with the existing technological scheme of the treatment plant and do not endanger the life and health of the personnel serving it, taking into account the specific conditions and with:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the permit for the discharge of wastewater, issued under the procedure of this Act;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the quantity, type and degree of pollution of the wastewater;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the capacity and efficiency of the existing sewerage network and treatment plant;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the technology for sludge treatment in view of its further utilization or final disposal.
(2) Persons who discharge industrial wastewaters into the sewerage system of a populated area, under a contract with the person who has a permit for discharge, are obliged to send a copy of the contracts to the basin directorate.
(3) The director of the basin directorate may prescribe an amendment to the conditions of the contracts if he assesses that the norms for the discharge of industrial wastewaters into the sewerage systems of populated areas are violated, as well as when these norms are not violated, but there is a danger of destruction of the sewerage system and pollution of groundwaters.
(4) When, as a result of an unlawful or clearly ill-considered discharge of industrial wastewaters into the sewerage system, damages are caused to the environment or to the person who owns the sewerage system, the sewerage enterprise in whose favor the discharge permit is issued, and the person who discharged the industrial wastewaters, are jointly and severally liable for the damages caused.
(5) In case of proven violations of the conditions of the contract by the persons who discharge industrial wastewaters into the sewerage system of the populated area, the holder of the discharge permit may require the discharger of the wastewater to conduct, at his own expense, own monitoring after coordination with the director of the respective basin directorate.

**Art. 125a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The connection of new consumers discharging wastewater to the sewerage systems of populated areas, settlement and resort formations is prohibited in cases where the sewerage system cannot ensure the discharge and treatment of wastewater, in compliance with the conditions in the permit for the discharge of wastewater issued under this Act.

**Art. 126.** (1) The persons who carry out the operation of the sewerage networks and treatment facilities are obliged to maintain them in technical and operational good condition and to ensure their continuous normal operation.
(2) When carrying out planned prophylactic repair works of the facilities referred to in para. 1, as well as in case of need for changes in the treatment technology, the obligated persons shall notify the basin authorities in writing of these works at least 30 days before the start of the works.
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The bypass and emergency connections to the treatment plants, from which a discharge into surface waters can be made, are sealed in a closed state by the Regional Inspectorate of Environment and Water (RIEW). Violation of the seals is allowed after notification and consent of the RIEW.

**Art. 127.** (1) When designing, constructing, reconstructing, modernizing and expanding industrial enterprises, sewerage systems of populated areas and other facilities, the necessary facilities for wastewater treatment are simultaneously designed, constructed, rebuilt and expanded.
(2) The commissioning of facilities and the carrying out of activities without accepted in the established order treatment facilities are prohibited, except in cases where they are not necessary.
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The bypass and emergency connections to the treatment plants are designed and provided with shut-off facilities, and when they discharge into surface waters, they are sealed under the conditions of Art. 126, para. 3.
(4) (New - SG, No. 44 of 2020, in force from 14.05.2020) The treatment plants for wastewater of populated areas, settlement and resort formations are provided with treatment facilities/installations for disinfection. Disinfection is carried out before discharge into surface waters and the Black Sea when necessary, at the discretion of the authorities of the Ministry of Health. Mandatory disinfection is carried out before discharge into the Black Sea during the tourist season.

**Art. 136.** The ministers referred to in Art. 135, item 11, issue instructions for the indicators that determine the best available technologies for the protection of waters from the activities for which they are responsible.

**Chapter Nine.**
**PROTECTION FROM THE HARMFUL EFFECTS OF WATERS**

**Section I.**
**General provisions (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010)**

**Art. 137.** (1) (Previous text of Art. 137 - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Protection from the harmful effects of waters includes:
1. protection from floods;
2. protection from ice phenomena;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) protection of the beds and banks of rivers from erosion;
4. protection of the banks from wave action;
5. protection from a dangerous rise or fall of the groundwater level;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 78 of 236

6. protection of river basins from water erosion;
7. protection from artificial self-outflow of groundwaters;
8. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) protection from sea-induced floods of coastal areas.
(2) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Floods can be:
1. natural floods, which are caused mainly by the melting of ice and snow, by precipitation or by the formation of ice jams or freezing;
2. man-made floods, which are caused by other influences - by damage to a hydrotechnical facility, which may lead to an accident, or by preventing critical situations in a hydrotechnical facility.

**Art. 138.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The protection under Art. 137 is operational and permanent.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 93 of 2009, in force from 25.12.2009, amend. - SG, No. 53 of 2014) Operational protection consists in carrying out the activities under Art. 19, para. 1 of the Disaster Protection Act and is carried out by the Unified Rescue System.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 93 of 2009, in force from 25.12.2009, suppl. - SG, No. 80 of 2011, in force from 14.10.2011, amend. - SG, No. 53 of 2014) Operational protection is carried out in accordance with the emergency plans under Art. 138a and the disaster protection plans under Art. 9 of the Disaster Protection Act.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) Permanent protection includes the activities assigned to the performer of the obligation to provide public services for protection from the harmful effects of waters and:
1. (suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) construction and maintenance of dikes, river and gully corrections and other hydrotechnical and protective facilities;
2. creation and maintenance of systems for observation, forecasting and warning;
3. regulation of the groundwater level in case of its dangerous rise or fall;
4. activities for the protection of river basins from water erosion;
5. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) maintenance of the conductivity of riverbeds;
6. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) construction and maintenance of strengthening and/or coastal protection facilities along the sea coast for protection against wave action;
7. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010, suppl. - SG, No. 80 of 2011, in force from 14.10.2011, amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015, in force from 01.01.2016) application of measures to prevent and limit the damages caused by natural floods, carried out in accordance with the flood risk management plans;
8. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015, in force from 01.01.2016) implementation of measures for

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 79 of 236

maintenance of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities in good technical condition and ensuring their safe operation;
9. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015, in force from 01.01.2016, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) implementation of activities for decommissioning of dam walls and/or their appurtenant facilities, which are in a pre-emergency state, until the restoration of their technological and structural safety or the liquidation of such dam walls and/or facilities, if their restoration or reconstruction are inexpedient;
10. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010, former item 8 - SG, No. 58 of 2015, in force from 01.01.2016) maintenance of navigation conditions on the Danube River.
(5) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) Permanent protection under para. 4 is carried out:
1. within the boundaries of populated areas - by the competent authorities under Art. 140, para. 4;
2. outside the boundaries of populated areas:
a) when providing public services for protection from the harmful effects of waters - by the performer of the obligation within the boundaries of his assigned territories;
b) by the competent authorities under Art. 140, para. 5 in the other cases.

**Art. 138a.** (New - SG, No. 80 of 2011, in force from 14.10.2011, amend. - SG, No. 53 of 2014) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The owners or users of water management systems and facilities and of the sites under Art. 131, para. 1 prepare emergency plans under the procedure of Art. 35 of the Disaster Protection Act or assign their preparation to operators, ensuring the implementation of the measures provided for therein. The emergency plans contain:
1. brief technical data on the systems or facilities;
2. assessment of the possible causes for the occurrence of emergency situations:
a) passage of a high wave with a security lower than the design one;
b) seismic impacts;
c) terrorist act;
d) increased filtration or water leakage, unusual displacements, deformations, cracks, slope slips and others;
e) a major accident in another facility;
3. assessment of the maximum possible consequences for the site, the environment, the population and the infrastructure after it - endangered populated areas, industrial and other sites;
4. measures to limit and eliminate the consequences of emergency situations;
5. measures for the protection of personnel;
6. activation of the emergency plan, distribution of duties and responsible structures and persons for the implementation of the provided measures;
7. readiness time for reaction of the structures and persons under item 6;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 80 of 236

8. resources and means necessary for the implementation of the provided measures;
9. action in emergency situations;
10. action in case of an accident in a separate facility;
11. physical security of the sites and facilities and action in case of a signal for a terrorist act;
12. systems for notification and redundancy of the power supply and the means of communication;
13. procedure for informing the executive authorities in case of need to introduce the disaster protection plans.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The specific requirements for the format and content of the emergency plans of the dams are determined by the ordinance under Art. 141, para. 2.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The regional governors appoint commissions, which once a year carry out inspections for the readiness for safe operation of the dams and their appurtenant facilities under Art. 141b, para. 1, items 1 and 2, and for those under Art. 141b, para. 1, item 3 - once every three years. The commissions:
1. analyze the provided information under Art. 141, para. 6 and carry out on-site inspections of the technical condition of the dam walls and their appurtenant facilities;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) check the established organization for the implementation of the requirements and measures provided for in the emergency plan;
3. check the implementation of the activities for ensuring the conductivity of the riverbed at a distance of up to 500 m from the dam walls;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) give a conclusion on the readiness for safe operation of the dam and its appurtenant facilities in normal, extreme and emergency conditions, based on the opinion of each member of the commission;
5. (new - SG, No. 55 of 2018) in connection with the conclusion under item 4, give instructions to the owners of the dams to bring them into readiness for safe operation of the dams and their appurtenant facilities in normal, extreme and emergency working conditions, incl. for carrying out repairs and other technical activities to bring the dam wall and its appurtenant facilities into good technical condition, as well as determine a deadline for their implementation;
6. (new - SG, No. 55 of 2018) draw up a protocol on the inspection carried out, containing the conclusion under item 4 and the instructions under item 5, within 14 days of the inspection under item 1, which they provide to the regional governor for approval and send a copy of it to: the owner of the dam, the Chief Directorate "Fire Safety and Civil Protection" of the Ministry of Interior, the mayor of the municipality on whose territory the dam is located, the chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance and the director of the respective basin directorate.
(4) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The commissions under para. 3 include representatives of:

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

1. (in force from 01.01.2016) the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance;
2. the Chief Directorate "Fire Safety and Civil Protection" of the Ministry of Interior;
3. the respective regional administration;
4. the respective basin directorate;
5. (new - SG, No. 55 of 2018) the respective municipality on whose territory the dam is located.
(5) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) The persons under para. 4 must have the necessary professional qualification for carrying out the activities under para. 3, and at least one of them must have a higher education with a "Master" degree in one of the specialties of the professional field "Architecture, Civil Engineering and Geodesy", related to the design, construction and operation of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities.
(6) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The regional governor may attract additional experts with the appropriate qualifications to participate in the commissions under para. 3.

**Art. 138b.** (New - SG, No. 80 of 2011, in force from 14.10.2011, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) In case of a dispute or ambiguity regarding the ownership of a dam, the state enterprise under Art. 139a carries out its organization and technical operation until the entry into force of the court decision or until the owner is established in compliance with the requirements of Art. 138c, para. 1.

**Art. 138c.** (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) (1) (Suppl. - SG, No. 17 of 2021) If the owner of a dam and its appurtenant facilities does not meet the requirements for a dam wall operator within the meaning of this Act, he shall mandatorily assign the management, maintenance and carrying out of the technical operation of the dam wall and its appurtenant facilities to a person who meets these requirements. When the owner grants a concession for the dam, Art. 20, para. 5 shall apply.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 17 of 2021) If the lessee of a dam and its appurtenant facilities meets the requirements for a dam wall operator, the owner may assign to him the performance of these functions by the lease agreement.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The operator of a dam wall and its appurtenant facilities, determined under the procedure of para. 1 or 2, is obliged to provide the necessary assistance to the owner for the fulfillment of his obligations under Art. 138a, para. 3, item 5, Art. 141, para. 1 and Art. 190a, para. 2, as well as to perform his assigned duties in accordance with the normative requirements and with the care of a good manager.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The operator of a dam wall is obliged to

take actions within its competence for the implementation of the instructions given under the procedure of Art. 138a, para. 3, item 5 and Art. 190a, para. 1, item 3.
(5) The obligations and responsibilities of the dam wall operator, as well as the procedure and manner in which he will carry out his activities, are determined in the ordinance under Art. 141, para. 2.

**Art. 139.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 80 of 2011, in force from 14.10.2011, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The maintenance and repair-restoration activities of dams, hydrotechnical and protective facilities are provided by the owners.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The persons under para. 1 ensure the maintenance and conductivity of the riverbed, dikes, river and gully corrections and other hydrotechnical and protective facilities in accordance with the parameters of the spillway facilities at a distance of up to 500 m from the dam walls.
(3) When other persons also benefit from the facilities under para. 1, they owe a part of the expenses in proportion to the received or expected benefits.
(4) When the permit for the construction of the facilities under para. 1 is issued after the actual establishment of an activity that suffers damages from the construction and operation of the facilities, their owner is obliged to compensate for the damages caused.

**Art. 139a.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) (1) A State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams" is established with the status of a state enterprise within the meaning of Art. 62, para. 3 of the Commercial Act, hereinafter referred to as "SEMOD".
(2) The State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams" is a legal entity with its registered office in Sofia. The enterprise is not a commercial company and does not form and distribute profit.
(3) The main object of activity of SEMOD is the complex management of dams - public and private state property.
(4) The State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams" carries out other activities that ensure or supplement the main object of activity.
(5) The state provides SEMOD with property - public and private state property, determined by a decision of the Council of Ministers, for the fulfillment of its object of activity.
(6) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) The dams whose ownership the municipalities have transferred free of charge to the state are managed by the State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams".
(7) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) Outside the scope of activity of SEMOD are the dams that are managed and operated by "National

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 83 of 236

Electric Company" - EAD, "Irrigation Systems" - EAD, "Zeminvest" - EAD, WSS operators with state or with state and municipal participation in the capital.
(8) The activity of SEMOD for the fulfillment of the tasks related to the main object of activity is financed by:
1. revenues from the activity;
2. a transfer from the state budget;
3. other receipts determined by a normative act.
(9) The funds under para. 8 are spent for the implementation of the object of activity and the maintenance of SEMOD.
(10) The structure and activity of SEMOD are regulated by a rulebook adopted by the Council of Ministers.

**Art. 139b.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) (1) Annually by March 1, SEMOD submits to the Ministry of Economy an activity plan for the current calendar year and an annual report on the activity for the previous calendar year.
(2) The plan under para. 1 includes the activities under Art. 139a for the respective year and contains at least the following elements:
1. goals and expected results;
2. activities to be carried out to achieve the results, including an investment plan of the enterprise;
3. a plan for the management of funds developed on the basis of expected expenses and revenues from the activity of the enterprise.
(3) The Minister of Economy approves the activity plan of SEMOD and the annual report under para. 1, which are public.
(4) The funds for administrative expenses of SEMOD are approved by the Minister of Economy simultaneously with the plan under para. 1.
(5) The funds and operations of SEMOD are included in the consolidated fiscal program as funds and operations of other economically separate entities under Art. 13, para. 4 of the Public Finance Act and are not part of the state budget.

**Art. 139c.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) (1) The State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams" is managed by a management board.
(2) The State Enterprise "Management and Operation of Dams" is represented by an executive director.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 103 of 2018, in force from 13.12.2018) The management board of SEMOD consists of 7 members, including a chairman.
(4) The members of the management board are:
1. chairman - the Minister of Economy or a deputy minister designated by him;
2. a representative of the Ministry of Environment and Water;
3. a representative of the Ministry of Regional Development and

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

Page 84 of 236

Public Works;
4. a representative of the Ministry of Agriculture, Food and Forestry;
5. a representative of the Ministry of Energy;
6. a representative of the National Association of Municipalities in the Republic of Bulgaria (NAMRB);
7. the executive director.
(5) The members of the management board and the executive director of SEMOD are appointed by the Minister of Economy upon the proposal of the respective minister or the management board of NAMRB.
(6) The members of the management board may not carry out, in their own name or on behalf of another, a competing activity and may not be in contractual relations with other enterprises, companies and associations with a similar subject of activity.
(7) A person may not be a member of the management board if he/she is:
1. convicted of a crime of a general nature;
2. a spouse or a relative in a direct line, in a collateral line or by affinity up to the third degree inclusive with another member of the management board.
(8) The management contract with a member of the management board is terminated before the expiration of its term when the person:
1. does not meet the requirements of the law;
2. violates or fails to fulfill the conditions provided for in the law or in the management contract;
3. has submitted a written request for release;
4. by decision of the Minister of Economy - with one month's notice;
5. upon withdrawal of the nomination of the representative.
(9) In the cases under para. 7 or upon the death of a member of the management board, the Minister of Economy appoints a new one and concludes a contract with him.
(10) The management board may take decisions if at least half of its members are present in person or are represented by another member of the board. A present member may not represent more than one absent member. For representation, an explicit power of attorney is required for each specific case.
(11) The decisions of the management board are taken by a simple majority.
(12) The management board may take decisions also in absentia if all members have stated their written consent for the decision.

**Art. 139d.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The decisions of the management board of SEMOD for the expenditure of financial resources are public and are published on the website of the Ministry of Economy within 14 days of their adoption.

**Art. 139e.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018, suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2019, in force from 02.08.2019) In carrying out its activities, SEMOD has the rights and obligations of the owner of the dam walls and their appurtenant facilities on

(11) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) When exercising control over the implementation of the activities under Art. 138, para. 4, the authorities under para. 2 give mandatory instructions and, if necessary, request the assistance of the bodies of the Ministry of Interior, of state and municipal bodies and of legal and natural persons.
(12) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The activities for cleaning riverbeds, organized and carried out by the performer of the obligation to provide public services for protection from the harmful effects of waters, in accordance with Art. 138, para. 5, are carried out in a volume and on territories, in accordance with the obligations assigned under this Act, and are controlled and coordinated by the Ministry of Agriculture, Food and Forestry. When carrying out planned or emergency activities related to maintaining the conductivity of rivers, gullies and drainage facilities, the performer shall notify in advance or at the first opportunity in case of an emergency situation the respective territorial structures of the regional administration,

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 88 of 236

the basin directorate and, in case the cleaning includes the removal of plantations, the Executive Agency for Forestry, with respect to which para. 9 is applicable.

**Art. 141.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The owners of water management systems and hydrotechnical facilities, including dam walls and/or their appurtenant facilities, are obliged to ensure:
1. their maintenance in good technical condition;
2. (in force from 01.01.2016, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) the use of measuring and control equipment for monitoring their condition, which meets the requirements of the ordinance under para. 2;
3. (in force from 01.01.2016, amend. - SG, No. 101 of 2015, in force from 22.12.2015) the use of an information system provided by the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance, in accordance with an ordinance issued by the Minister of Economy upon a proposal from the chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance;
4. compliance with the requirements for technical and safe operation of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities, determined in the ordinance under para. 2;
5. regulation of the water levels in the dams in order to reduce the risk of flooding.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 108 of 2001, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 36 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 82 of 2009, in force from 16.10.2009, amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014, amend. - SG, No. 14 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The conditions and procedure for the implementation of the technical and safe operation of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities and for the implementation of control over their technical condition are determined by an ordinance of the Council of Ministers upon a proposal from the chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance.
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010, rep. - SG, No. 58 of 2015)
(4) (Previous para. 3 - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The obligations under para. 1 also apply to the owners of reservoirs whose degree of siltation no longer allows for their further use for their intended purpose. In this case, the owner prepares and implements a reclamation project.
(5) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The owners of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities are obliged to notify in writing the chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance:
1. of the designated operator of the dam wall and its appurtenant facilities - before the commissioning of newly built dam walls and their appurtenant facilities;
2. of each choice or change of the operator of the dam wall and its appurtenant facilities - within 7 days of the change;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

Page 89 of 236

3. of the results of the periodic inspections under the procedure of the ordinance under para. 2.
(6) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The information under para. 5, item 3 is also sent to the respective regional governor for the needs of the commission under Art. 138a, para. 3.

**Art. 141a.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) (1) Depending on their size - the height of the dam wall and the volume of the reservoir, large dams are those that meet at least one of the following conditions:
1. dams with a wall height greater than 15 m, measured from the lowest point of the foundation to the crest of the dam;
2. dams with a height between 5 m and 15 m, impounding a volume greater than 3 million cubic meters.
(2) Small dams are dams that do not meet the conditions under para. 1.
(3) Control under the procedure of this Act and the ordinance under Art. 141, para. 2 is subject to all dams under paras. 1 and 2, with the exception of small dams for which, during their classification with regard to their potential hazard, it has been established that a breach of the structural integrity of their walls does not pose a threat to human life or endanger critical infrastructure and they meet at least one of the following conditions:
1. the created water head is less than 7.0 m and the impounded volume is less than 50,000 cubic meters;
2. the created water head is less than 2.0 m regardless of the impounded volume;
3. the impounded volume is less than 15,000 cubic meters regardless of the created water head;
4. its catchment basin is not more than 2.0 sq.km and the reservoir is not filled by diversions or a pumping station.
(4) The owners are responsible for the technical good condition and safe operation of the dams under para. 3. They are not obliged to assign the management, maintenance and carrying out of the technical operation of the dam wall and its appurtenant facilities to a person who meets the requirements for a dam wall operator.

**Art. 141b.** (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) (1) Dams are classified into three degrees of potential hazard depending on the worst possible consequences of the release of the water stored in the dam due to failure or improper operation of the dam:
1. first high degree of potential hazard;
2. second significant degree of potential hazard;
3. third low degree of potential hazard.
(2) The criteria for classifying the degree of potential hazard under para. 1 are determined in the ordinance under Art. 141, para. 2 by an interdepartmental commission appointed by the Council of Ministers, which includes representatives of the Ministry

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 90 of 236

of Environment and Water, the Ministry of Regional Development and Public Works, the Ministry of Agriculture, Food and Forestry, the Ministry of Energy, the Ministry of Economy, the Ministry of Interior and the scientific community, having a direct relation to dam walls and their appurtenant facilities.
(3) The commission under Art. 138a, para. 3 classifies the dams by degree of potential hazard in accordance with the ordinance under Art. 141, para. 2.

**Art. 142.** (Suppl. - SG, No. 81 of 2000, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 93 of 2009, in force from 25.12.2009) When releasing water from hydrotechnical facilities during the passage of high waves, in emergency conditions or when carrying out repair works, the owner or user of the same shall notify in advance the respective municipal administrations, basin directorates and the bodies of the Ministry of Interior, and for transboundary rivers - also the border police.

**Art. 143.** To protect against the harmful effects of waters, the following are prohibited:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) disturbance of the natural state of the beds, the banks of rivers and the coastal floodplains;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) reduction of the conductivity of riverbeds, including by weirs and sills, without the respective permit;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) the use of riverbeds as landfills for waste, earth and rock masses;
4. the construction of structures over covered river sections;
5. the storage or stockpiling of materials that would significantly increase the destructive force of the water during floods.

**Art. 144.** (1) (Previous text of Art. 144 - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The following are prohibited on dikes:
1. passage with vehicles outside the designated places for this;
2. cultivation and disturbance of their surface;
3. placing of poles or signs;
4. planting of trees and shrubs;
5. passage of domestic animals outside the designated places for this;
6. construction of wells or fishponds;
7. disposal of waste and other materials and objects.
(2) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The following is prohibited on earthfill dam walls

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 91 of 236

the performance of the activities under para. 1, items 2, 3, 4, 6 and 7.

**Art. 145.** (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) (1) In case of danger of flooding, which may cause adverse consequences for the life and health of people, the environment and material values, which can be prevented or limited by the destruction of a hydrotechnical facility or part of it, the owner and the person who manages the facility are obliged to provide full assistance to the mayor of the municipality on whose territory the facility is located, for carrying out the necessary works on the facility to prevent or limit the expected damages.
(2) The activities under para. 1 are carried out by order of the mayor of the respective municipality, in coordination with the regional governor and the head of the territorial unit of the Chief Directorate "Fire Safety and Civil Protection".
(3) The funds spent for carrying out the activities under para. 1, as well as for the restoration of dikes, if they have been destroyed under the procedure of para. 1, are restored by a decision of the Interdepartmental Commission for Recovery and Assistance at the Council of Ministers.
(4) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) Within 14 days of the implementation of the activities under para. 1, the mayor of the respective municipality is obliged to notify the chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical Surveillance of the destruction of the hydrotechnical facility or part of it.

**Art. 146.** (1) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, suppl. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The placement of residential and villa buildings and farm buildings in the floodplains of rivers and the servitude of hydrotechnical facilities and dam walls is prohibited.
(2) The basin directorates notify the authorities that issue permits for the construction of residential, villa and farm buildings of the location and scope of the coastal floodplains of rivers.

**Section II.**
**Preliminary flood risk assessment (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010)**

**Art. 146a.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) For each river basin management district under Art. 152, para. 1, including the Bulgarian part of the Danube River, a preliminary flood risk assessment is carried out according to the methodology under Art. 187, para. 2, item 6.
(2) The assessment under para. 1 includes:

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 92 of 236

1. maps of the river basin management districts on an appropriate scale, indicating the topography and land use, including the boundaries of:
a) river basins and sub-basins;
b) coastal areas - where such exist;
2. a description of past floods with significant adverse consequences for human health, the environment, cultural heritage, technical infrastructure and economic activity and for which it can be expected that they will be repeated in the future;
3. the scale of the floods, their path of propagation and an assessment of their adverse consequences;
4. an assessment of the potential adverse consequences of future floods for human health, the environment, cultural heritage, technical infrastructure and economic activity, taking into account, as far as possible:
a) the topography, the location of the watercourses and their general hydrological and geomorphological characteristics, including retention lowlands as natural water-retaining surfaces;
b) the effectiveness of man-made infrastructures (systems and facilities) for flood protection, the location of populated areas, areas of economic activity and long-term public works;
c) the impact of climate change on the occurrence of floods.

**Art. 146b.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010, until 22.12.2010) (1) A preliminary flood risk assessment under Art. 146a, para. 1 is not carried out for river basins or sub-basins when:
1. it has been established on the basis of a risk assessment started before 22 December 2010 that there is or is likely to be a significant potential risk of flooding;
2. before 22 December 2010, decisions have been issued for the preparation of flood hazard maps, flood risk maps and for the development of flood risk management plans that meet the requirements of this Act.
(2) The assessment under para. 1, item 1 is carried out by the director of the respective basin directorate.
(3) The decisions under para. 1, item 2 are issued by the director of the respective basin directorate.

**Art. 146c.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) For the international river basin management districts, the Republic of Bulgaria ensures the exchange of up-to-date information necessary for the preliminary flood risk assessment through the respective basin directorate for water management.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 93 of 236

**Art. 146d.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The director of the basin directorate carries out the preliminary assessment under Art. 146a, para. 1 and determines areas for which there is:
1. a significant potential risk of flooding;
2. a probability of a significant potential risk of flooding.
(2) The areas under para. 1 are determined for each river basin management district or for a part of an international district in accordance with Art. 151, para. 2, item 2, letter "t" and are approved by the Minister of Environment and Water.

**Section III.**
**Flood hazard maps and flood risk maps (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010)**

**Art. 146e.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) For the areas determined under Art. 146b, para. 1, items 1 and 2 and Art. 146d, para. 1, the following are prepared:
1. flood hazard maps, and
2. flood risk maps.
(2) The preparation of maps in accordance with para. 1 for areas under Art. 146b, para. 1, items 1 and 2 and Art. 146d, para. 1, which are common with other countries, is carried out after a preliminary exchange of information between the respective countries.

**Art. 146f.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The flood hazard maps cover areas that may be flooded in case of:
1. floods with a low probability of occurrence, where the probable period for recurrence is greater than or equal to 1000 years, as well as in case of unforeseen events;
2. floods with a medium probability of occurrence, where the probable period for recurrence is greater than or equal to 100 years;
3. floods with a high probability of occurrence, where the probable period for recurrence is greater than or equal to 20 years, where appropriate.
(2) The maps for each of the probability periods under para. 1 show the following elements:
1. the extent of the flood;
2. the depth or level of the water;
3. where appropriate - the flow velocity or the corresponding water quantity.
(3) For areas under threat of flooding caused by groundwaters, the maps under para. 1, item 1 are prepared.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 94 of 236

**Art. 146g.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The flood risk maps show the adverse consequences of floods for each of the probability periods under Art. 146e, para. 1, expressed through the following indicators:
1. the approximate number of potentially affected inhabitants;
2. the type of economic activity in the potentially affected area;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the installations in Appendix No. 4 to Art. 117 of the Environmental Protection Act, which may cause additional pollution due to an accident in case of flooding, and the water protection zones under Art. 119a, para. 1, items 1, 2 and 5, for which there is a possibility of being affected;
4. other significant sources of pollution not specified in item 3.

**Art. 146h.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The maps under this section are prepared according to the methodology under Art. 187, para. 2, item 6, are updated and reviewed by the director of the respective basin directorate.
(2) The flood hazard maps and the flood risk maps are reviewed and updated every 6 years simultaneously with the analyses and review under Art. 156h, item 2.
(3) The preparation of the first flood hazard maps and flood risk maps and their subsequent reviews are carried out in such a way that the information contained in them is consistent with the information under Art. 157, items 1, 3 and 4.

**Section IV.**
**Flood risk management plans (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010)**

**Art. 146i.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) Based on the maps under Art. 146e, flood risk management plans are prepared at the level of the river basin management district for the areas under Art. 146d, para. 1, as well as for the areas under Art. 146b, para. 1, item 2.
(2) When developing the plans under para. 1, the information and data for the development of the river basin management plans are used.

**Art. 146k.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The first flood risk management plans contain:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the conclusions of the preliminary flood risk assessment in accordance with the requirements of Section I of this chapter in the form of a summary map of the river basin management district, outlining the areas defined under Art. 146d, para. 1, which are the subject of this management plan

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 95 of 236

of flood risk;
2. the flood hazard maps and the flood risk maps, developed in accordance with Section II of this chapter, and the conclusions that can be drawn from these maps;
3. a description of the flood risk management objectives, determined in accordance with para. 2, item 1;
4. a brief presentation of the measures and their priority, aimed at achieving the flood risk management objectives, including the measures taken in accordance with para. 2, item 2, and the measures regarding floods, required and taken in accordance with other normative acts in the field of environment, related to:
a) environmental impact assessment and ecological assessment of plans and programs;
b) water protection in case of major industrial accidents;
c) the river basin management plan and the achievement of the environmental protection objectives under Art. 156a.
(2) The flood risk management plans also include:
1. objectives for:
a) reducing the potential adverse consequences of floods for human health, the environment, cultural heritage, technical infrastructure and economic activity;
b) reducing the probability of flooding;
2. measures to achieve the objectives under item 1;
3. a description of the implementation of the plan.

**Art. 146l.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The description of the implementation of the plan under Art. 146k, para. 2, item 3 includes:
1. a description of the priorities and the manner of monitoring the progress of the implementation of the plan;
2. a summary of the public information and the measures and/or actions taken for consultation;
3. a list of the competent authorities and, where appropriate, a description of the consultation process in any international district and of the consultation process with the river basin management plan.

**Art. 146m.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) When developing the flood risk management plans, the following are taken into account:
1. the cost/benefit assessment;
2. the extent and path of propagation of the floods;
3. the areas that have the potential to retain water during floods, such as natural floodplains;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 96 of 236

4. the objectives under Chapter Ten, Section III;
5. the management of soils and waters;
6. spatial planning;
7. land use;
8. the protection of:
a) nature;
b) infrastructure related to navigation and ports;
9. the characteristics of the river basin or sub-basin in accordance with the river basin management plans.
(2) The flood risk management plans address all aspects of risk management, focusing on:
1. flood prevention;
2. flood protection;
3. increasing preparedness for flooding, including flood forecasts;
4. establishing an early warning system.
(3) Flood risk management plans may also include the promotion of sustainable land use practices, improving water retention, as well as controlled flooding of certain areas in case of flooding.
(4) Flood risk management plans may not contain measures which, by their scale and impact, significantly increase the risk of flooding for other countries upstream or downstream of the river - for international river basins, unless these measures are agreed with the respective country and a common solution has been found in accordance with Art. 146n.

**Art. 146n.** (New - SG, a No. 61 of 2010) (1) For each river basin management district or for a part of an international river basin management district, a common flood risk management plan is prepared.
(2) When the flood risk management plan is for a part of an international river basin that falls entirely within the territory of the European Union, it is coordinated with the respective Member States in cases where a common flood risk management plan is not prepared for the entire international river basin.
(3) When the flood risk management plan is for a part of an international river basin that does not fall entirely within the territory of the European Union, the plan is coordinated with the respective countries, if possible, in cases where a common flood risk management plan is not prepared for the entire international river basin.

**Art. 146o.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The flood risk management plans

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 97 of 236

are reviewed and updated every 6 years.
(2) The update of the plan contains:
1. changes or updates from the publication of the previous version of the flood risk management plan, including a summary of the reviews carried out in accordance with this section;
2. an assessment of the progress in achieving the objectives under Art. 146k, para. 2, item 1;
3. a description and explanation of all measures provided for in the earlier version of the flood risk management plan that were planned but not undertaken;
4. a description of all additional measures from the publication of the previous version of the flood risk management plan.
(3) The first flood risk management plans are developed in coordination with the update of the river basin management plans under Art. 159 within the period under ยง 138, para. 2 of the transitional and final provisions of the Act Amending and Supplementing the Water Act (prom., SG, No. 65 of 2006; corr., No. 66 of 2006; amend., No. 22 of 2007, No. 95 of 2009) and are included in them.

**Section V.**
**Public information (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010)**

**Art. 146p.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) In the development, review and updating of the flood risk management plans, as well as of the preliminary assessment, the decisions and the assessment under Art. 146b and of the maps under Section II of this chapter, information is provided to the public about the planned measures and the results achieved from their implementation.

**Art. 146q.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) For each river basin management district, the following are published and announced to the public, including water users, for consultation and written opinions:
1. a draft of the preliminary assessment and/or the assessment under Art. 146b;
2. a draft of the maps under Section II of this chapter and the proposals for amendment and updating;
3. a draft of a flood risk management plan, including the planned measures and the expected results of their implementation, as well as the achieved results and the proposals for amendment and updating of the measures and the plan.
(2) The information is provided to the public as follows:
1. under para. 1, item 1 - three and a half years before the beginning of the period to which the flood risk management plan relates;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 98 of 236

2. under para. 1, item 2 - two and a half years before the beginning of the period to which the flood risk management plan relates;
3. under para. 1, item 3 - within the time limits under Art. 168b, para. 2, item 3.
(3) The information under para. 1 is published on the website of the respective basin directorate and on the website of the Ministry of Environment and Water.
(4) The notice that the information under para. 1 has been announced is published in two national daily newspapers and in the electronic mass media.
(5) Upon request, access is provided to the documents and information used for the development of the respective projects under para. 1.

**Art. 146r.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The projects are announced to the public for opinions:
1. for a period of two months - for the projects under Art. 146q, para. 1, items 1 and 2;
2. in accordance with the time limits under Art. 168c, para. 1 - for the projects under Art. 146q, para. 1, item 3.
(2) Any person may, within the period under para. 1, consult the respective basin directorate regarding the documents under Art. 146q, para. 1 and submit a written opinion.
(3) The opinions under para. 2 are an integral part of the documentation for the flood risk management plans, as well as for the preliminary assessment, the decisions and the assessment under Art. 146b and of the maps under Section II of this chapter.

**Art. 146s.** (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The provisions of Art. 146q and 146r also apply to the review and/or updating of:
1. the flood risk management plans;
2. the preliminary assessment, the decisions and the assessment under Art. 146b;
3. the maps under Section II of this chapter.
(2) During the reviews and/or updates in accordance with para. 1, the probable consequences of climate change on the risk of flooding are taken into account.

**Chapter Ten.**
**WATER MANAGEMENT**

**Section I.**
**General provisions**

**Art. 147.** (Rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 99 of 236

**Art. 148.** (1) Water management is carried out at the national and basin level.
(2) The river basin districts are determined by the natural location of the watersheds between the catchment areas of one or several main rivers on the territory of the Republic of Bulgaria.
(3) The river basins defined by this Act do not follow the administrative-territorial division of the country and are a basis for environmental management on a basin principle.
(4) (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) When a river basin management district includes a transboundary watercourse, this district belongs to an international river basin management district.
(5) (Previous para. 4 - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The management of water management systems is carried out on a technological and basin principle in accordance with the conditions of the permits for use and protection of waters and water bodies.

**Art. 148a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) The Republic of Bulgaria participates in the development and coordination jointly with other countries of policies, programs and strategies for the protection of transboundary waters on the basis of the principles under Art. 2a, item 4.
(2) The Republic of Bulgaria, jointly with the other countries, ensures:
1. coordination for the development of unified management plans for international river basins that fall entirely within the territory of the European Union, and ensuring the achievement of good water status in the Bulgarian part of the international river basin management districts;
2. the implementation of the requirements of Art. 156a - 156g and of the programs of measures within the international river basin management districts.
(3) The provision of para. 2, item 1 applies where possible and when the international river basins do not fall entirely within the territory of the European Union, and when the impossibility of the plan is established, it applies in the Bulgarian part of the international river basin management districts.
(4) The implementation of the activities under paras. 1 and 2 may be carried out within existing structures established by virtue of international agreements, and if necessary, for the implementation of the requirements of para. 2, item 2 - with the assistance of the European Commission.
(5) Representatives of the Republic of Bulgaria in the international commissions coordinating the activities under paras. 1 and 2 are officials designated upon a proposal from the Minister of Environment and Water.
(6) (Rep. - SG, No. 44 of 2020, in force from 14.05.2020)

**Art. 149.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The management

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 100 of 236

of waters, water bodies and water management systems and facilities is carried out on the basis of river basin management plans.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 21 of 2020, in force from 13.03.2020) The plans under para. 1 are public and are linked with other plans within the respective territorial level, including with the integrated territorial strategies for the development of the planning regions of level 2, the spatial development, forestry, park management and other plans.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Plans that are not in conformity with this Act and with the river basin management plans may be amended by the Council of Ministers upon a proposal from the Minister of Environment and Water.

**Art. 149a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) When developing the management plans under Art. 149, the following are determined:
1. environmental protection objectives;
2. waters intended for drinking and domestic water supply;
3. zones for water protection;
4. programs of measures.
(2) When developing the river basin management plans, a characterization of the river basin management district is carried out.

**Section II.**
**Water management bodies**

**Art. 150.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The state policy for water management is carried out by the Minister of Environment and Water, and in the cases under Art. 148a, para. 1 - jointly with the Minister of Foreign Affairs.
(2) Drafts of international treaties, as well as of other international acts, such as declarations, programs and memoranda, which concern the waters of the Bulgarian territory and their management, are coordinated under the procedure of the International Treaties Act.

**Art. 151.** (1) (New - SG, No. 18 of 2005, in force from 20.01.2005) The National Assembly adopts a National Strategy for the Management and Development of the Water Sector, which determines the main goals, stages, means and methods for the development of the water sector.
(2) (Previous text of Art. 151, suppl. - SG, No. 18 of 2005, in force from 20.01.2005) For management at the national level:
1. The Council of Ministers:

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 101 of 236

a) (rep. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)
b) (suppl. - SG, No. 36 of 2006, in force from 01.07.2006) grants a concession for the extraction of mineral waters - exclusive state property;
c) (suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) adopts national programs in the field of protection and sustainable use of waters, annual reports and the necessary measures for their implementation;
d) permits the use of waters for the purposes of the defense and security of the country;
e) (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) determines restrictions on the use of waters in case of unforeseen or exceptional circumstances affecting certain regions of the country;
f) (amend. - SG, No. 70 of 2004, in force from 01.01.2005) determines the quantity of mineral waters under Art. 14, item 2 for use by medical institutions for hospital care upon a reasoned proposal from the Minister of Health;
g) determines the tariffs for the fees collected on the grounds specified in this Act;
h) (new - SG, No. 18 of 2005, in force from 20.01.2005) proposes for approval by the National Assembly a National Strategy for the Management and Development of the Water Sector;

2. the Minister of Environment and Water:
