**Section III.**
**Environmental protection objectives (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)**

**Art. 156a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The objectives under Art. 149a, para. 1, item 1 for environmental protection with respect to the quantity and quality of waters are determined for:
1. surface waters for:
a) preventing the deterioration of the status of all surface water bodies;
b) protecting, improving and restoring all surface water bodies to achieve a good status of the waters;
c) protecting and improving the quality of waters in all artificial and heavily modified water bodies and achieving a good ecological potential and good chemical status of the surface waters;
d) preventing, progressively reducing and ceasing at once or in stages the pollution from emissions, discharges and losses of priority and priority hazardous substances;
2. groundwaters for:
a) preventing or limiting the discharge of pollutants into groundwaters and preventing the deterioration of the status of all groundwater bodies;
b) protecting, improving and restoring all groundwater bodies, ensuring a balance between groundwater abstraction and recharge and achieving their good status;
c) (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) identifying and reversing any significant and sustained upward trend in the concentration of any pollutant with the aim of continuously reducing groundwater pollution;
3. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the zones for water protection under Art. 119a to achieve the objectives of the legislation by virtue of which the zone is determined or declared.
(2) The measures and deadlines for achieving the environmental protection objectives

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 110 of 236

under para. 1 are determined by the river basin management plans.
(3) In cases where more than one of the objectives under para. 1 are set for a single water body, the most stringent one is adopted.

**Art. 156b.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) A surface water body may be designated as artificial or heavily modified when:
1. (suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the changes in the hydromorphological characteristics of the water body that would be necessary to achieve good ecological status may have significant adverse effects on:
a) the environment;
b) navigation, port facilities and recreational areas;
c) the activities for the carrying out of which impoundment for drinking and domestic water supply, irrigation or electricity production is necessary;
d) the regulation of waters, flood protection, land drainage;
e) other activities equally important for sustainable development;
2. (suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the benefits of the artificial or heavily modified characteristics of the water body cannot be achieved by other means, which are a significantly better ecological option, due to technical infeasibility or economic unreasonableness.
(2) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The designation of the bodies under para. 1, as well as the reasons and grounds for the designation of each water body, and their updating are carried out every 6 years with the river basin management plans.

**Art. 156c.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The deadlines under Art. 156a, para. 2 may be extended with the updating of the river basin management plans for the phased achievement of the environmental protection objectives in cases where the deterioration of the status of the affected water body has been stopped and the following conditions are met:
1. the competent authority establishes that it is impossible to achieve an improvement in the status of the water bodies within the specified period under Art. 156a, para. 2, when:
a) the necessary improvements can be achieved only in stages for a longer period for reasons of a technical nature;
b) improving the status of the water bodies within the specified period is economically unreasonable;
c) natural conditions do not allow for the improvement of the status of the water body within the specified period;
2. in the river basin management plan are indicated:
a) the extension of the period and the reasons for it are justified;
b) the planned measures for the phased bringing of the water bodies into the planned

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 111 of 236

status within the period under item 3, a schedule for their implementation, as well as the reasons for any significant delay;
3. the extension is for a period not longer than two subsequent updates of the river basin management plan, except in cases where natural conditions do not allow for the achievement of the objectives within this period;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) in the river basin management plan or its update are included:
a) a list of the measures that are planned as necessary for the gradual achievement of the required status of the water body within the extended period;
b) a justification for the reasons for the delay in the implementation of these measures and the expected deadlines for their implementation;
c) a review of the implementation of these measures within the previous plan and a list of all additional measures that must be implemented during the current plan period.

**Art. 156d.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The environmental protection objectives may be less stringent for specific water bodies when, during the analysis and review under Art. 156h, items 1 and 2, it is established that they have been significantly affected by human activity or that their natural conditions are such that the achievement of the environmental protection objectives under Art. 156a, para. 1 is impossible or economically unreasonable and when the following conditions are met:
1. the ecological and socio-economic needs provided by such activity cannot be met by such means, guaranteeing a significantly better environmental protection at comparable costs;
2. there are impacts that could not have been avoided due to the nature of the human activity or pollution and have been achieved:
a) the best possible ecological and chemical status for surface waters;
b) the smallest possible changes in the good status of groundwaters;
3. no further deterioration in the status of the waters in the affected water body occurs;
4. the reasons for determining less stringent environmental protection objectives are specified in the river basin management plan and these objectives are subject to review every 6 years.

**Art. 156e.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) A temporary deterioration of the status of water bodies is not considered a violation of this Act when it is a result of natural causes or unforeseeable or exceptional circumstances, including severe floods and prolonged droughts, or is a result of circumstances caused by

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 112 of 236

incidents that could not have been foreseen, in cases where:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) all practical measures have been taken to:
a) prevent future deterioration of the status of the water body;
b) not to impede the achievement of the objectives of this Act for other water bodies not directly affected by these circumstances;
2. in the river basin management plan, the circumstances that may be defined as unforeseen or exceptional are indicated;
3. the measures for implementation in the event of unforeseen or exceptional circumstances are included in the program under Section V and will not prevent the restoration of the status of the water body after the cessation of these circumstances;
4. (suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) the consequences of these circumstances are reviewed annually, and in the cases under Art. 156c, item 1, all practical measures are taken for the fastest possible restoration of the status of the water body to its state before these circumstances;
5. in the next update of the river basin management plan, a brief review of the consequences of these circumstances, of the measures taken and planned in accordance with items 1 and 4, is included.

**Art. 156f.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) There is no violation of this Act in cases where:
1. good ecological status of surface waters or good ecological potential of heavily modified water bodies is not achieved or their status is prevented from deteriorating as a result of a new modification of the physical characteristics of the surface water body;
2. the prevention of deterioration of the status of a surface water body - from excellent to good, is not achieved as a result of new activities for sustainable human development with socio-economic effect;
3. good status of groundwaters is not achieved or their status is prevented from deteriorating as a result of a change in their level.
(2) In the cases under para. 1, it is required:
1. that all practical measures be taken to reduce the adverse impact on the status of the water body;
2. the reasons for the established changes or deviations to be explicitly stated and explained in the river basin management plan and the objectives to be reviewed every 6 years;
3. the reasons for these changes or deviations to be in the public interest or the benefits thereof for human health and safety or for sustainable development to outweigh the benefits for the environment and for society from achieving the objectives under Art. 156a, para. 1;
4. the benefits achieved with these changes or deviations in the status of the

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 113 of 236

water body, due to technical reasons or excessive costs, cannot be achieved by other means, the implementation of which is more environmentally friendly.
(3) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The programs of measures under Art. 156n, para. 2, item 1, letter "a" shall plan measures related to an environmental impact assessment for activities that may lead to the failure to achieve good status or potential of the respective water body or to the deterioration of its status, related to:
1. a new modification of the physical characteristics of surface water bodies;
2. abstraction of surface waters when:
a) the sum of the project water quantity and the already permitted water abstractions exceeds 60 percent of the permanent freshwater resources with a 95-percent security for the basin of the respective river;
b) when abstracting the project water quantity and the already permitted other abstractions, there is a risk that the minimum permissible flow in the river will not be guaranteed during the low-water period of the river;
3. abstraction of groundwater through existing or through new water abstraction facilities when:
a) the permitted abstraction from the water body exceeds 60 percent of the available groundwater resources for the previous year;
b) the monitoring of the levels shows a lowering of the water levels at the monitoring points.
(4) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The programs of measures under Art. 156n, para. 2, item 1, letter "a" shall plan measures related to an environmental impact assessment for:
1. all new activities in water bodies in which the status is lower than good and the respective activity is the pressure that contributes to this, including the construction of dams and hydroelectric power plants, abstraction of surface and groundwater;
2. water bodies for which exceptions under para. 1 have been applied in the previous river basin management plan.
(5) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) In the cases under paras. 3 and 4, when the investment proposal falls within the scope of Annex No. 2 to the Environmental Protection Act, when assessing the need to carry out an environmental impact assessment, the following are taken into account:
1. the implementation of the requirements under para. 2;
2. the alternative solutions under para. 7 for the respective investment proposal.
(6) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The assessment of the cumulative impact of all already permitted activities within the boundaries of the water body is taken into account in the cases under paras. 3 and 4 - for each investment proposal.
(7) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) For each investment proposal,

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 114 of 236

falling within the scope of paras. 3 and 4, an assessment of the implementation of the requirements under para. 2, including for each alternative solution, is included, by:
1. considering the proposed measures to reduce the adverse impact on the status of the water body and other components of the environment related to it;
2. assessing the benefit to society or to human health and safety, or for sustainable development and comparing it with the benefits for the environment and for society from achieving a good status of the waters;
3. assessing other possible options for achieving the benefits of the investment proposal, which are technically feasible and do not require excessive costs and which will not lead to changes or deviations in the status of the water body, and justifying the reasons why an alternative leading to such changes and deviations has been chosen.
(8) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) When the activities under paras. 3 and 4 do not fall within the scope of Annex No. 1 and Annex No. 2 to the Environmental Protection Act, the assessments under para. 7 are carried out within the framework of the ecological assessment of the river basin management plans.
(9) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The specific criteria for carrying out the assessments under paras. 6 - 8 are determined by a methodology for the application of the exceptions under Art. 156b - 156e, approved by the Minister of Environment and Water.
(10) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The assessments under paras. 6 - 8 are included in the river basin management plans as a justification for the applied exceptions under para. 1.

**Art. 156g.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) (1) When applying the provisions of Art. 156b - 156e:
1. a permanent planning of exceptions and compromises in achieving a good status of other water bodies within the river basin management district is not allowed;
2. compliance with the requirements for the application of other national acts and the acts of the European Union in the field of environment is ensured.
(2) The provisions of Art. 156b - 156e shall apply:
1. only to individual water bodies determined in the river basin management plan, provided that the achievement of the objectives of this Act for other water bodies is not impeded;
2. in such a way as to ensure compliance with national acts and the acts of the European Union in the field of environmental protection.

**Section IV.**

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 115 of 236

**Characterization of the river basin management district (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)**

**Art. 156h.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) For each river basin management district or for the part of an international district, the following are carried out:
1. an analysis of its characteristics,
2. a review of the impact of human activity on the status of surface and groundwater, and
3. (amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) an economic analysis of water use under Art. 192, para. 2, item 1.

**Art. 156i.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The analysis under Art. 156h, item 1 is carried out under the conditions and procedure specified in the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 2 and the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 9.
(2) When carrying out the analysis under para. 1, the following are determined:
1. surface and groundwater bodies;
2. heavily modified and artificial surface water bodies;
3. the types of surface water bodies for each category:
a) rivers;
b) lakes;
c) transitional waters;
d) coastal waters;
4. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015) barrier facilities that disrupt the continuity of rivers.

**Art. 156k.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The review of the impact under Art. 156h, item 2 includes the determination of the water bodies for which there is a risk of not meeting the set environmental protection objectives.

**Art. 156l.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The information under Art. 156h - 156k is reviewed and, if necessary, updated every 6 years after the first update.

**Section V.**
**Programs of measures for the protection and restoration of waters (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)**

**Art. 156m.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For each river

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 116 of 236

basin management district and for each part of an international river basin management district, a program of measures is developed, taking into account the analyses under Section IV and the objectives under Section III.
(2) The Minister of Environment and Water may determine measures that are applicable in all river basin management districts and/or for the parts of the international river basin management districts.

**Art. 156n.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Each program includes basic and, if necessary, supplementary measures.
(2) The basic measures ensure the implementation of the minimum mandatory requirements and include:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) the measures necessary for the implementation of this Act, the subordinate normative acts for its implementation and other normative acts in the field of environment related to waters, including the measures required for:
a) the application of the combined approach for point and diffuse sources, of the environmental impact assessment procedures and of the integrated pollution control;
b) the protection of waters intended for drinking and domestic purposes and of bathing waters;
c) the protection of birds and habitats;
d) the protection of waters from pollution with nitrates, with plant protection products and in case of major industrial accidents;
e) the treatment of wastewater from populated areas and the treatment and utilization of wastewater sludge;
2. the measures that ensure the application of the principle of fuller recovery of the costs of water services, including the resource and environmental protection costs;
3. measures to promote the efficient and sustainable use of waters to achieve the environmental protection objectives under Section III;
4. measures for the protection of waters for drinking and domestic water supply, including measures for the protection of their quality in order to reduce the degree of treatment for obtaining water of drinking quality;
5. regulation of the abstraction of fresh surface and ground waters, the impoundment of fresh surface waters, which includes:
a) issuance of permits for water abstraction;
b) entry of the permits under letter "a" in the registers under Art. 182 and 183;
c) periodic review and updating of the regulation;
6. (suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) regulation of the artificial recharge of groundwaters for the restoration or increase of groundwater resources

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 117 of 236

bodies, which includes:
a) (suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) issuance of a permit for artificial recharge of groundwaters, where the source of the water used for artificial recharge may be any surface or groundwater body, the quality of which does not compromise the achievement of the defined environmental protection objectives of the groundwater body whose resources are being restored or increased through recharge;
b) (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) periodic review and updating of the permit;
7. regulation of emissions by determining prohibitions on the introduction of pollutants from point sources of pollution or requirements for the issuance of permits and their periodic review and updating;
8. determination of prohibitions on the introduction of pollutants from diffuse sources of pollution and measures for the prevention or regulation of pollution, including by introducing requirements for cases where such are not regulated in national legislation, as well as their periodic review and updating;
9. (suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) measures to prevent and reduce all other significant adverse impacts on the state of the waters, established during the review under Art. 156h, item 2, in order to ensure compatibility between the hydromorphological conditions in the water bodies and the achievement of the required ecological status or good ecological potential for water bodies designated as artificial or heavily modified, including the issuance and review, and if necessary - the ex officio amendment or termination of the permits under Art. 44 for surface water abstraction and the permits for the use of a water body under Art. 46, para. 1;
10. measures to stop the pollution of surface waters with priority substances and to gradually reduce the pollution with other substances that may prevent the achievement of the environmental protection objectives for surface water bodies, determined in Art. 156a;
11. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) other measures to prevent significant losses of pollutants from technical installations and to prevent and/or reduce the impact of accidental pollution as a result of floods, which include:
a) systems for detecting or warning of such events;
b) all appropriate measures to reduce the risk to aquatic ecosystems in cases of unforeseen accidents;
12. (new - SG, No. 61 of 2010) specific measures to achieve a good chemical status of groundwaters and to protect them from pollution and deterioration, determined by the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 2.

1. legislative measures;
2. administrative measures;
3. economic and/or financial measures;
4. environmental agreements;
5. emission control measures;

**Art. 156o.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) When data from monitoring or other data show that the environmental protection objectives for a given water body cannot be achieved through the provided measures and/or within the set period, additional measures are planned for it to achieve these objectives, including:
1. investigation of the reasons for the possible non-fulfillment;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) review and, if necessary, amendment of the issued permits;
3. review and, if necessary, amendment of the monitoring programs;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) where necessary, the taking of other measures, including the establishment of more stringent quality standards than those determined in the ordinances under Art. 135, para. 1, items 2, 9 and 17, including individual emission limits under the procedure of the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 13.
(2) When the reasons under para. 1, item 1 are a result of exceptional and unforeseen circumstances, incl. floods and prolonged droughts, under the conditions of Art. 156d, additional measures may not be implemented.

**Art. 156p.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The implementation of the programs of measures may not, directly or indirectly, lead to an increase in the pollution of surface and marine waters, as well as of the environment.

**Art. 156q.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The programs of measures are developed within the framework of the river basin management plans.
(2) The programs are reviewed and, if necessary, depending on the results achieved, are updated every 6 years.
(3) All new or reviewed measures reflected in the updated program are implemented within three years of their approval.

**Section VI.**
**River basin management plans (Previous Section III, title amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)**

**Art. 157.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, former text of Art. 157 - SG, No. 61 of 2010) River basin management plans are developed for each river basin management district and contain:
1. a general description of the characteristics of the river basin management district in accordance with Section IV, including:
a) for surface waters:
aa) maps with the location and boundaries of the surface water bodies;
bb) maps of the ecoregions and the types of surface water bodies;
cc) determination of the reference conditions for the types of surface water bodies;
b) for groundwaters, maps with the location and boundaries of the groundwater bodies;
2. a brief overview of the significant types of pressure and impact as a result of human activity on the status of surface and groundwater, including:
a) an assessment of pollution from point sources;
b) an assessment of pollution from diffuse sources, including a review of land use;
c) an assessment of the impact on the quantity of waters, including abstractions;
d) an analysis of other impacts as a result of human activity on the state of the waters;
3. a list and maps of the zones for water protection;
4. maps of the monitoring networks of surface waters, groundwaters and

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

of the zones for water protection;

7. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) a brief overview of the economic analysis of water use;

**Section VII.**
**Public information and consultation (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)**

**Art. 168a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) In the development, review and updating of the river basin management plans, information is provided to the public about the planned measures and the results achieved from their implementation.

**Art. 168b.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For each river basin management district, the following are published and announced to the public, including water users, for consultation and written opinions:

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 123 of 236

1. a timetable and work program for the development of the river basin management plan and the public discussions that need to be held;
2. an interim review of the identified problems related to water management;
3. a draft river basin management plan.
(2) The information under para. 1 is provided to the public:
1. under item 1 - at least three years before the beginning of the period to which the plan relates;
2. under item 2 - at least two years before the beginning of the period to which the plan relates;
3. under item 3 - at least one year before the beginning of the period to which the plan relates.
(3) The information under para. 1 is published on the website of the respective basin directorate and on the website of the Ministry of Environment and Water.
(4) The notice that the information under para. 1 has been announced is published in two national daily newspapers and in the electronic mass media.
(5) In the cases under para. 1, item 3, upon request, access is provided to the documents and information used for the development of the draft river basin management plan.

**Art. 168c.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The documents under Art. 168b, para. 1 are announced to the public for opinions for a period of 6 months.
(2) Any person may, within the period under para. 1, consult the respective basin directorate regarding the documents under Art. 168b, para. 1 and submit a written opinion.
(3) The opinions under para. 2 are an integral part of the documentation for the river basin management plan.

**Art. 168d.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) When updating the river basin management plan, the provisions of Art. 168b and 168c shall apply.

**Section VIII.**
**Monitoring of waters and of water protection zones (Previous Section IV, title amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006)**

**Art. 169.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The monitoring of waters and of water protection zones ensures a coherent and comprehensive overview of the state of the waters in each river basin management district.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 124 of 236

(2) The monitoring is carried out according to programs approved by the Minister of Environment and Water, developed by the basin directorates in accordance with the specifics of the water bodies and their characteristics.
(3) The review under para. 1 and the programs under para. 2 are part of the national environmental monitoring system.

**Art. 169a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the monitoring of surface waters, programs for surveillance, operational and, if necessary, investigative monitoring are developed.
(2) The programs for monitoring of surface waters include:
1. hydrological and morphological observations, including volume, water quantity and water level to determine the ecological and chemical status and the ecological potential of the water body;
2. observations of the ecological and chemical status and the ecological potential.

**Art. 169b.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the monitoring of groundwaters, programs for surveillance and operational monitoring are developed.
(2) The programs for monitoring of groundwaters include observations of the chemical and quantitative status of the groundwater body.

**Art. 169c.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the zones for water protection, the programs under Art. 169a and 169b are supplemented with observations related to the specifics of the zone, determined in the law and in the act for its establishment.
(2) The zones for water protection, characterized as water bodies at risk, are included in the programs for operational monitoring of surface and groundwaters.
(3) In the cases under para. 1, monitoring is also carried out on the factors affecting the state of these water bodies, including the impact caused by the implementation of the programs of measures.
(4) The monitoring under para. 1 continues until the objectives for environmental protection set by the river basin management plan are achieved for the specific zone for water protection.

**Art. 170.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The water monitoring networks are:

para. 1, item 14.

**Art. 174.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) Persons to whom rights for water abstraction or use of water bodies have been granted are obliged to conduct own monitoring in accordance with the requirements of the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 14 and the conditions in the issued permits for:
1. the quantity and quality of the waters;
2. the quantity of wastewater and the concentration of the emitted pollutants.
(2) The persons under para. 1 shall store the information from the measurements made for a period of 6 years.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The authorities under Art. 52, para. 1, items 1 and 4, when exercising their control functions, have the right of access at any time to the monitoring devices and facilities and to the information under para. 2.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Upon termination of the right of water abstraction and/or use of the water body, the information under para. 2 is handed over to the respective basin directorate for storage.
(5) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The persons under para. 1 shall annually by March 31 provide the director of the basin directorate, and in cases of a permit issued under Art. 46, para. 1, item 3, letter "b" and of a complex permit - also to the director of the RIEW, the results of the implementation in the previous year of own monitoring within the framework of the report on the implementation of the conditions in the permits under Art. 48, para. 1, item 12.

**Art. 175.** (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, former text of Art. 175 - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The data from the observations and assessments obtained as a result of water monitoring, as well as of own monitoring, are the basis for exercising control and for imposing sanctions in case of violation of the normative requirements.
(2) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The directors of the basin directorates include the data from the own monitoring when carrying out the assessments of the state of the water bodies and of the effectiveness of the implemented measures provided for in the river basin management plans.
(3) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The data from the own monitoring and the results of the control carried out on the parameters of the permitted use of waters are the basis for determining the fees for water abstraction, for the use of a water body and for water pollution.

**Chapter Eleven.**
**FINANCIAL ORGANIZATION AND ECONOMIC REGULATION**

**Art. 192.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) Economic regulation is based on the following principles:
1. cost recovery for water services, including those for the environment and for the resource;
2. the polluter pays.
(2) For the purposes of economic regulation:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 23.06.2009) an economic analysis of water use is developed;
2. a pricing policy is implemented which provides appropriate incentives for consumers for the efficient use of waters in view of achieving the environmental protection objectives;
3. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015) fees for water abstraction, for the use of a water body and for pollution are determined, as an element of the recovery of resource costs and environmental costs and ensuring the contribution of the various water users to the recovery of water service costs.
(3) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The implementation of the principles under para. 1 is carried out, taking into account the economic analysis under para. 2, item 1, developed in accordance with Art. 192a.

**Art. 192a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) The economic analysis under Art. 192, para. 2, item 1 is developed for each river basin management district and contains:
1. an assessment of the contribution of the various water users, distributed at least into the categories of industry, agriculture and households, to the recovery of the costs of water services;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 138 of 236

2. full and detailed information on the recovery of the costs of water services, taking into account the long-term forecasts for the supply and demand for water, and when necessary, and:
a) an assessment of the quantities, prices and costs associated with water services;
b) an assessment and forecast of the necessary investments;
3. an assessment of the most cost-effective combination of measures to be included in the program under Section V.
(2) When determining the scope of the information under para. 1, the costs of collecting the relevant data are also taken into account.

**Art. 192b.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The pricing policy under Art. 192, para. 2, item 2, the fees under Art. 192, para. 2, item 3 and the assessment under Art. 192a, para. 1, item 1 take into account the social and economic effect and the effect for environmental protection from the cost recovery, as well as the geographical and climatic conditions in the respective regions.

**Art. 192c.** (1) (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, former text of Art. 192c - SG, No. 61 of 2010) The measures to ensure the pricing policy under Art. 192, para. 2, item 2 and the contribution of water users under Art. 192a, para. 1, item 1 are included in the river basin management plans.
(2) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010) An adequate contribution from the various water users, distributed at least into the categories of industry, agriculture and households, to the recovery of the costs of water services is ensured, taking into account the economic analysis of water use and the "polluter pays" principle.

**Art. 193.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) Public relations related to water supply and sewerage services are regulated by the Act on the Regulation of Water Supply and Sewerage Services, in compliance with the requirements of this Act.

**Art. 194.** (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) For the right to use waters, the following are paid:
1. a fee for water abstraction from:
a) surface waters;
b) groundwaters;
c) mineral waters;
2. a fee for the use of a water body for:
a) (amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) extraction of alluvial deposits from the Danube River

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

Page 139 of 236

and reservoirs;
b) (rep. - SG, No. 36 of 2008)

3. (amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) a fee for pollution:
a) for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters;

c) industrial enterprises outside the cases under letter "b" - as a sum of:
aa) the fee determined on the basis of the annual load by chemical oxygen demand for the industrial wastewaters discharged into the surface water body, with correction coefficients depending on the number of priority hazardous, priority and specific substances, and
bb) the fee for domestic wastewaters, determined on the basis of the annual quantity of discharged domestic wastewaters into the surface water body;

(amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2017, in force from 18.07.2017) under letter "c" - with an ordinance of the Council of Ministers, upon a proposal from the Minister of Agriculture, Food and Forestry, in coordination with the Minister of Environment and Water, which determines the amount, the procedure and manner of calculation and payment of the fees.

(7) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The fee under para. 5:
1. item 1:
a) letter "a" is included in the recognized annual costs forming the necessary annual revenues of the WSS operators;
b) letter "d" is not included in the recognized annual costs forming the necessary annual revenues of the WSS operators, but is paid individually by the consumers through the WSS operator providing the "wastewater discharge" service;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018) item 3 is paid:
a) individually by the owner or user of the farm - for the fees for diffuse pollution from animal husbandry and aquaculture;
b) by the person who places fertilizers and plant protection products on the market.
(8) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) If the permit holder builds and operates a system for continuous automated monitoring and when the system's readings are validated by the controlling authority, the fee under para. 1, item 3, letter "a" is determined on the basis of the actual loads of the polluting substances.
(9) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) For the recovery of environmental and resource costs, a correction coefficient is determined for increasing the fee:
1. for water abstraction - in case of individual water supply (through own water abstraction facilities);
2. for pollution:
a) in water bodies whose chemical or ecological status is lower than good;
b) in water protection zones;
c) when discharging into drying, karst and sinking rivers, as well as into small and medium-sized rivers, determined in the ordinance under Art. 135, para. 1, item 9.
(10) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The fee under para. 1, item 2, letter "d" is due until

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

the commissioning of the facility ensuring the continuity of the river.
(11) (Previous para. 7, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The fee under para. 1 is not paid in the cases:

2. of firefighting;
3. when the water abstraction is for the purpose of drainage;
4. (new - SG, No. 36 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2018, in force from 27.11.2018, amend. - SG, No. 25 of 2019) of water abstraction for aquaculture under Art. 44 and of use for aquaculture under Art. 46, para. 1, item 2 of a water body for aquaculture and related activities;

8. (new - SG, No. 58 of 2015) for the extraction of alluvial deposits in the cases under Art. 140.

(13) (New - SG, No. 61 of 2010, former para. 9 - SG, No. 58 of 2015) When the competent authorities establish that in the condition of the main system to the facility where mineral water is used, damages have occurred that prevent the exercise of the granted right of water abstraction, and the system is not the property of the permit holder, the water abstraction fee is determined on the basis of the abstracted water volume, the conditions of Art. 194a, para. 1 and the temperature of the mineral water for the period from the date of establishing the damage until the restoration of the main system, but not more than one year for the duration of the permit.

**Chapter Eleven "a".**
**MANAGEMENT, PLANNING AND CONSTRUCTION OF WSS SYSTEMS. PROVISION OF WSS SERVICES. UNIFIED INFORMATION SYSTEM FOR WSS SERVICES. REGISTRATION OF WSS ASSOCIATIONS AND WSS OPERATORS (NEW - SG, NO. 47 OF 2009, IN FORCE FROM 24.09.2009)**

**Chapter Eleven "a" MANAGEMENT, PLANNING AND CONSTRUCTION OF W and S SYSTEMS. PROVISION OF W and S SERVICES. UNIFIED INFORMATION SYSTEM FOR W and S SERVICES. REGISTRATION OF W and S ASSOCIATIONS AND W and S OPERATORS (NEW - SG, NO. 47 OF 2009, IN FORCE FROM 24.09.2009)**

**Section I.**
**Management of water supply and sewerage systems (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009)**

**Art. 198a.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The territory of the country for the purposes of management, planning and construction of WSS systems and for the provision of WSS services is divided into consolidated territories.
(2) The boundaries of the consolidated territory may change depending on the accession or withdrawal of municipalities from it.
(3) The decisions to change the boundaries of the consolidated territory are taken by the general meeting of the WSS association or by the municipal council.
(4) A consolidated territory ceases to exist when the municipalities in it join another consolidated territory.
(5) The decision to terminate the existence of a consolidated territory and to join the municipalities from it to another consolidated territory is taken by the general meeting of the WSS association or by the municipal council.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 147 of 236

**Art. 198b.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) The management of the WSS systems is carried out by:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works, who coordinates the management of the WSS systems at the national level;
2. the WSS association, in which the state and one or more municipalities participate - when the ownership of the WSS systems within the boundaries of the consolidated territory is distributed between the state and the municipalities or between several municipalities;
3. the municipal council - when the WSS systems within the boundaries of the consolidated territory are the property of only one municipality.

**Art. 198c.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The WSS association under Art. 198b, item 2 is a legal entity with a registered office and address in the regional administration of the respective consolidated territory.
(2) The WSS association is not a commercial company, does not form and does not distribute profit.
(3) The management bodies of the WSS association are:
1. a general meeting, which consists of representatives of the state and the municipality/municipalities, determined under Art. 198e, paras. 1 - 3;
2. a chairman, who is a representative of the state.
(4) The WSS association through the general meeting:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 96 of 2017, in force from 02.01.2018) determines the WSS operator under the procedure of this Act or sends representatives to the commission that conducts the procedure for determining a concessionaire under the procedure of the Concessions Act;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 103 of 2013) adopts a decision to conclude a contract on behalf and for the account of the owner of the WSS system with the WSS operator for the assignment of activities for the provision of the WSS service and the maintenance of the WSS systems, including for the assumption of financial obligations by the WSS operators, and controls the implementation of the contract;
3. prepares and adopts the regional master plan of the WSS systems and facilities and the master plan of agglomerations over 10,000 e.p. of the WSS systems of the respective consolidated territory;
4. prepares and adopts a long-term and short-term investment program for the regional master plan of the WSS systems and facilities and a long-term investment program for the master plan of agglomerations over 10,000 e.p. of the WSS systems and facilities of the respective consolidated territory;
5. coordinates the business plan of the WSS operator;
6. (amend. - SG, No. 96 of 2017, in force from 02.01.2018) distributes among the owners the funds received from the WSS operator under the contract for the provision of WSS services, in accordance with the percentage ratio of their votes, when there is more than one owner of the WSS systems;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 148 of 236

7. adopts decisions to change the boundaries of the consolidated territory;
8. adopts a decision to terminate the existence of the consolidated territory and to join the municipalities from it to another consolidated territory;
9. prepares and adopts its annual budget;
10. adopts the annual report on its activity.
(5) The chairman of the WSS association:
1. organizes and manages its activities and represents it;
2. signs the contract with the WSS operator and other contracts on behalf of the WSS association;
3. organizes the implementation of the decisions of the general meeting of the WSS association;
4. approves the job description, concludes, amends and terminates the employment contracts of the employees of the WSS association;
5. (amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) annually by the end of January submits a report on the activity of the WSS association for the previous year to the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works;
6. organizes the control over the implementation of the contracts with the WSS operators;
7. performs other functions assigned to him by the rulebook on the organization and activity of the WSS association under Art. 198e, para. 7.
(6) The meetings of the general meeting of the WSS association are convened by its chairman.
(7) (Amend. - SG, No. 103 of 2013, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The meetings are regular if the representatives of the state and the municipalities who hold at least two-thirds of all votes are present.
(8) When the state and more than one municipality participate in the respective WSS association, the state has the right to 35 percent of the votes, and all municipalities distribute among themselves 65 percent of the votes, in proportion to the number of their population.
(9) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The decisions of the general meeting of the WSS association are taken by a majority of three-quarters of the votes of those present under para. 7, with the exception of the decisions to change the boundaries of the consolidated territory, which are taken unanimously.
(10) When the state and one municipality participate in the respective WSS association, the decisions are taken unanimously.
(11) The activities of the WSS associations are assisted by employees appointed under the procedure of the Labour Code.
(12) The funds necessary for the activities of the WSS association are provided by the state and by the municipalities in accordance with the percentage ratio of their votes.
(13) (Amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) The funds under para. 12 are at the expense of the budget of

the Ministry of Regional Development and Public Works and of the budgets of the municipalities.

**Art. 198e.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The WSS association or the municipal council may oblige the WSS operator to assume financial obligations for securing funds for the development of the WSS systems when:
1. such a possibility is provided for in the contract with the WSS operator;
2. the funds will be used for financing projects from the approved investment program for the regional master plans or for the master plans of agglomerations over 10,000 e.p.;
3. the financial condition of the WSS operator allows for the assumption and servicing of the obligations;

(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 17 of 2015, in force from 06.03.2015) Until the approval by the EWRC of the business plan with the obligations included in it, the WSS operator does not assume financial obligations under para. 1.

**Art. 198f.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) In the WSS association, one representative of the state and one representative of the municipalities included in the consolidated territory participate.
(2) The representative of the state in the WSS association is:

(5) The position and the mandate of the representative of the municipality for the meetings of the general meeting of the WSS association are coordinated in an order determined by the municipal council.
(6) (Amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) After each meeting of the general meeting of the WSS association, the regional governor informs in writing the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works, the Minister of Environment and Water and the municipal councils of the issues discussed and the decisions taken.
(7) (Amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) The organization and activity of the WSS associations are determined by a rulebook issued by the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works after coordination with the Minister of Environment and Water.

**Art. 198g.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009, amend. - SG, No. 103 of 2013) The granting of the management of the WSS systems and facilities - public state, respectively - public municipal property, to the WSS association in the respective consolidated territory is carried out under the procedure of this Act.

**Art. 198h.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) The WSS association or the municipal council has the right to free access to the information systems and documents of other state bodies and local self-government bodies, as well as of all institutions and bodies maintaining registers and information systems provided for by law, when the data from the information systems and documents concern the regulation of WSS services and ownership of WSS systems.

**Section II.**
**Planning the development of water supply and sewerage systems (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009)**

**Art. 198i.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The planning of the development of the WSS systems and facilities is carried out through:
1. regional master plans of WSS, and
2. master plans for WSS of agglomerations over 10,000 e.p.
(2) For one consolidated territory, there can be only one regional master plan and as many master plans of agglomerations as necessary.
(3) The plans under para. 1 are prepared for a period of 25 years.
(4) The regional master plan covers the entire consolidated territory and contains at least:
1. an analysis of the state and needs of the WSS systems and facilities of the respective territory;
2. an analysis of the price and quality of the provided WSS services in the consolidated territory and a forecast for the development of the WSS service with a view to satisfying consumers, reducing water losses and ensuring a good quality of the service with social affordability of the price;
3. goals and priorities for the development of the WSS systems and facilities in the consolidated territory, through which compliance with the law of the European Union and with the programs of measures planned in the respective river basin management plan for the collection, discharge and treatment of wastewater from urbanized territories is achieved;
4. populated areas over 10,000 e.p., for which master plans of agglomerations and a schedule for their adoption are prepared;
5. a long-term investment program for the implementation of the plan and a short-term investment program for the first 5-year period.
(5) The master plans of agglomerations cover only the respective agglomeration and contain at least:
1. an analysis of the state and needs of the WSS systems and facilities in the respective agglomeration;
2. an analysis of the price and quality of the provided WSS services in the consolidated

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 152 of 236

territory and a forecast for the development of the WSS service with a view to satisfying consumers, reducing water losses and ensuring a good quality of the service with social affordability of the price;
3. goals and priorities for the development of the WSS systems and facilities in the agglomeration, through which compliance with European legislation and with the programs of measures planned in the respective River Basin Management Plan for the collection, discharge and treatment of wastewater from urbanized territories is achieved;
4. a long-term investment program for the implementation of the plan and a short-term investment program for the first 5-year period.
(6) The master plans of agglomerations within a single consolidated territory are prepared in accordance with the regional master plan.

**Art. 198j.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The regional master plans and the master plans of agglomerations are prepared by the WSS association or by the municipal council.
(2) The regional master plans and the master plans of agglomerations under para. 1 are reviewed and analyzed and, if necessary, are updated at periods not longer than 5 years, under the procedure of this Act.

**Art. 198k.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) Before their adoption, the regional master plans, the master plans of agglomerations and the investment programs for them:
1. are subject to an ecological assessment under the procedure of the Environmental Protection Act;
2. are reviewed and coordinated with the competent basin directorate for water management, and when they cover the territory of more than one basin directorate for water management - with the Minister of Environment and Water;
3. are coordinated with the regional development councils, and when the respective consolidated territory falls on the territory of two or more administrative regions - with each regional development council.

**Art. 198l.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) When preparing the long-term investment programs for the implementation of the regional master plans and the master plans of agglomerations, the principle of a single price for the WSS service in the consolidated territory is observed.
(2) (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The principle under para. 1 is mandatory for the prices of the WSS services "supply of water to consumers and/or to other WSS operators" and "discharge of wastewater". The price for the WSS service "treatment

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 153 of 236

of wastewater" may be determined on a differentiated basis for groups of consumers depending on the degree of pollution in accordance with the procedure of the Act on the Regulation of Water Supply and Sewerage Services and the acts for its implementation.
(3) (Previous para. 2 - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The projects included in the investment program correspond to the goals, priorities and forecasts in the respective regional master plan or in the respective master plan of the agglomeration and the programs of measures in the respective river basin management plan.

**Art. 198m.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The WSS operator prepares a business plan on the basis of the investment programs for the regional master plans and the master plans of agglomerations.
(2) The business plan of the respective WSS operator is coordinated by the WSS association or by the municipal council. In case of non-compliance with the master plans, the investment programs and the assignment contracts, the WSS association or the municipal council returns it for revision with a reasoned opinion and instructions.
(3) The business plans of the WSS operators are approved under the procedure of the Act on the Regulation of Water Supply and Sewerage Services.

**Section III.**
**Construction of water supply and sewerage systems (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009)**

**Art. 198n.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The state and the municipalities assign the construction of WSS systems and facilities - public state or public municipal property, in accordance with the regional master plans and the master plans of agglomerations and the investment programs for them. The WSS operators may assign the construction of WSS systems and facilities if this is assigned to them in the contract for the provision of WSS services.
(2) The municipalities may also build facilities for water supply and sewerage that are in accordance with the municipal development plan, but are not in accordance with the plans and programs under para. 1, with the additional costs for their management, maintenance and operation not being included in the prices of the WSS services that the WSS operator forms in the consolidated territory. These additional costs are borne by the consumers of the WSS services that are provided through the constructed facility, with the WSS operators forming separate prices.
(3) The investment design and the construction of the WSS systems and facilities are carried out in accordance with the approved specialized WSS schemes for the development plans under Chapter Seven, Section III of the Spatial Development Act.

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 154 of 236

(4) During the construction of the WSS systems and facilities under para. 1, the conditions for the development of the land properties may not be worsened and the established manner of their permanent use may not be hindered. An exception is allowed under the procedure of the Spatial Development Act when there is no other technical possibility or another technical solution is clearly economically inexpedient.
(5) The construction of a WSS system or parts of it affecting or passing through sites related to the security of the country is allowed only as an exception and with a justified necessity.
(6) The exception under para. 5 is allowed by an order of the head of the department to which the affected site has been provided for management. The order also determines the procedure for access to the site during the study, design and construction of the WSS system or parts of it.
(7) When commissioning the WSS system under para. 5, the heads of the department to which the affected site has been provided for management and of the WSS operator determine the access regime for the WSS operator, which is mandatory when carrying out the activities of management and maintenance of the WSS system or the part of it located within the boundaries of the site.
(8) The design, construction, commissioning and maintenance of the WSS systems are carried out under the conditions and procedure of the Spatial Development Act and of this Act.

**Section IV.**
**Provision of WSS services. Management, maintenance and operation of WSS systems (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009)**

**Art. 198o.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The management, maintenance and operation of the WSS systems and facilities, as well as the provision of WSS services to consumers for a fee, are carried out by WSS operators under the procedure of this Act and of the Act on the Regulation of Water Supply and Sewerage Services.
(2) Within the boundaries of one consolidated territory, only one WSS operator may carry out the activities under para. 1, with the exception of the cases under para. 6.
(3) One WSS operator may carry out the activities under para. 1 in more than one consolidated territory.
(4) The WSS association, through its chairman, or the municipal council, through the mayor of the municipality, grants the respective WSS operator the right to carry out the activities under para. 1 by assignment under the procedure of this Act and of the Concessions Act for the sites specified in Art. 13, para. 1, items 5 - 7 and Art. 19, para. 1, item 4, letters "a" and "b" and para. 2.
(5) The WSS operator is a trader, a state or municipal enterprise - a legal entity, which has a contract concluded with the chairman of the WSS association or with the mayor of the municipality in accordance with a decision of the municipal council for management,

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 155 of 236

maintenance and operation of the WSS systems and the provision of WSS services within the boundaries of one or more consolidated territories, when the provision of WSS services is its main activity.
(6) Traders, state or municipal enterprises - legal entities, which provide services for the supply and treatment of water for drinking and domestic purposes, for public needs, for production, industrial and other activities of a commercial nature or activities for the treatment and discharge of wastewater and do not serve the entire consolidated territory, but individual consumers, carry out these services in accordance with the requirements of this Act and the Act on the Regulation of Water Supply and Sewerage Services. With regard to these consumers, they are considered WSS operators.
(7) The requirements and criteria for WSS operators are determined by an ordinance of the Council of Ministers.
(8) The ordinance under para. 7 also determines the professional and qualification requirements for the technical personnel of the WSS operators, as well as the conditions and procedure for conducting their training.

**Art. 198p.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) (Suppl. - SG, No. 103 of 2013) The assignment of the activities under Art. 198o, para. 1 is carried out by a contract under the procedure of this Act or under the procedure of the Concessions Act.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 96 of 2017, in force from 02.01.2018) The commission for conducting the procedure for determining a concessionaire for the WSS associations includes the chairman of the WSS association and representatives elected by the general meeting.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 103 of 2013) The WSS operators recognize in their balance sheet (statement of financial position) the property rights granted to them by the contracts under para. 1 over the WSS systems and facilities granted to them - public property, and accrue depreciation expenses for them under the procedure of the Accountancy Act. These depreciation charges are reinvested by the WSS operators in the infrastructure in accordance with the approved investment programs for their approved business plans.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 103 of 2013) The WSS operator fulfills its obligations under the contract under para. 1 until the moment the newly selected WSS operator starts providing the WSS service.
(5) (New - SG, No. 103 of 2013) The contract under para. 1 shall determine at least:
1. the scope of the activities and responsibilities of the WSS operator for the provision of WSS services;
2. the obligations of the WSS operator for the operation, maintenance and reconstruction of the WSS systems and facilities;
3. the investment obligations of the WSS operator for the construction of new WSS systems and facilities;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 156 of 236

4. the conditions and procedure for the provision to the WSS operator for operation of the newly built and the forthcoming to be built WSS systems and facilities in the consolidated territory;
5. the procedure for provision for operation of the WSS systems and facilities to the WSS operator;
6. the procedure for handing over the WSS systems and facilities by the WSS operator after the termination of the contract;
7. the criteria and indicators for exercising control over the activity of the WSS operator;
8. the term of the contract;
9. the responsibilities of the parties in case of non-fulfillment of the obligations under the contract;
10. the grounds and procedure for early termination of the contract;
11. (amend. - SG, No. 17 of 2015, in force from 06.03.2015) the conditions and procedure for assuming and repaying financial obligations of the current WSS operator on the respective consolidated territory as of the date of entry into force of this Act and which are included in its business plan approved by the EWRC;
12. the conditions under which the WSS operator continues its activity in accordance with its approved business plan and the general conditions for the provision of WSS services.
(6) (New - SG, No. 103 of 2013) The WSS operator of the respective consolidated territory accepts for operation the WSS systems and facilities with the respective documentation necessary for their operation.

**Section V.**
**Unified information system for WSS services. Register of WSS associations and WSS operators (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009)**

**Art. 198q.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009, amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014) To ensure publicity and transparency in the implementation of the activity for the provision of WSS services, the Ministry of Regional Development and Public Works creates and maintains:
1. a Unified Information System for WSS services, and
2. a register of WSS associations and WSS operators.

**Art. 198r.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009, amend. - SG, No. 15 of 2016) The Unified Information System for WSS services ensures:

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

Page 157 of 236

of the WSS operators, for the indicators for reducing water losses and for the other main indicators approved by the business plans of the WSS operators;

3. the possibility of making inquiries in the business plans.

**Art. 198s.** (New - SG, No. 47 of 2009, in force from 24.09.2009) (1) The WSS associations and the WSS operators are entered in the register under Art. 198q, item 2 by consolidated territories.
(2) The register under para. 1 contains information on:

h) other data determined by the ordinance under Art. 198x;
4. the persons under Art. 198o, para. 6, acting on the consolidated territory - name, registered office and address, management bodies;

**Chapter Twelve.**
**ADMINISTRATIVE-PENAL AND CIVIL LIABILITY**

**Art. 199.** (1) The Minister of Environment and Water may order compulsory administrative measures in cases of:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) emergency and disaster situations caused by actions or omissions of water users in the process of water abstraction and/or use of water bodies and operation of water management systems and facilities;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) the occurrence of an immediate danger of pollution, damage or destruction of the environment,

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 159 of 236

of people or of the property of the state, municipalities, natural or legal persons as a result of actions or omissions of water users;
3. (new - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) water abstraction from mineral waters without an issued permit or granted concession.
(2) The order under para. 1 shall specify the motives and the amount of the expenses for carrying out the necessary activities and measures.
(3) The expenses are paid by the persons who are obliged by law or by the permit to carry out the activities and measures under para. 2.
(4) (Amend. - SG, No. 91 of 2002, in force from 01.01.2003) The expenses under this article may be paid in advance with funds from the Enterprise for Management of Environmental Protection Activities, and after the entry into force of the order under para. 1, the obligated person is obliged to reimburse them.
(5) (Amend. - SG, No. 12 of 2009, in force from 01.01.2010) If the obligated person does not do so, the claim is subject to compulsory execution under the procedure of the National Revenue Agency Act.
(6) (Amend. - SG, No. 30 of 2006, in force from 12.07.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 77 of 2018, in force from 01.01.2019) The order under para. 1 may be appealed by the affected persons before the respective administrative court under the procedure of the Administrative Procedure Code.

**Art. 199a.** (New - SG, No. 81 of 2000) (1) When applying compulsory administrative measures, the Minister of Environment and Water:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) terminates the water abstraction and/or use of water bodies;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) stops the activities as a result of which the waters are polluted or the beds or banks of the rivers are destroyed;
3. stops the activities as a result of which public interests and/or acquired rights are violated.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The application of compulsory administrative measures is carried out by officials authorized by the Minister of Environment and Water through:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) sealing of the water abstraction facilities;
2. sealing of the sites from whose activities the waters are polluted;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) sealing of machines and facilities through which the beds or banks of rivers are destroyed.

**Art. 199b.** (New - SG, No. 58 of 2015, in force from 01.01.2016) (1) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The chairman of the State Agency for Metrological and Technical

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 160 of 236

Surveillance or an official authorized by him applies a compulsory administrative measure by ordering by order the temporary decommissioning of dam walls and their appurtenant facilities until they are brought into a state corresponding to the technical norms.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The application of a compulsory administrative measure is carried out in case of an immediate danger of loss of human life, damage or destruction of property and/or the environment, when the danger is a result of an action or omission of an owner, operator, concessionaire or lessee of a dam.
(3) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The temporary decommissioning of dams and their appurtenant facilities is carried out by completely emptying the dam's reservoir by:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 17 of 2021) the concessionaire, when the dam is under concession;
2. the lessee, when the dam is leased;
3. the owner, when the grounds under items 1 and 2 are not present.
(4) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The order under para. 1 determines the obligated person and the costs for applying the measure.
(5) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) In case of non-compliance with the order by which a compulsory administrative measure is applied, the temporary decommissioning of the dam and its appurtenant facilities is carried out by the regional governor at the location of the dam.
(6) (New - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The costs for applying the compulsory administrative measure are at the expense of the persons under para. 3. When in the cases under para. 5 the obligated person does not reimburse the costs incurred, the claim is subject to compulsory execution under the procedure of the National Revenue Agency Act.
(7) (Previous para. 3 - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The compulsory administrative measures under para. 1 for the dams in Appendix No. 1 to Art. 13, item 1 are applied by a decision of the Council of Ministers.
(8) (Previous para. 4, amend. - SG, No. 55 of 2018) The acts under paras. 1 and 7 may be appealed by the affected persons under the procedure of the Administrative Procedure Code. The challenging of the acts under paras. 1 and 7 does not suspend their execution.

**Art. 200.** (1) A fine or a property sanction shall be imposed, unless subject to a more severe penalty, on the natural or legal person who:
1. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) uses water without the necessary grounds for this or in deviation from the conditions provided for in the permit or contract:
a) with a quantity of up to 1 l per second - from BGN 150 to BGN 1,000;
b) with a quantity from 1 l per second to 10 l per second - from BGN 500 to BGN 5,000;
c) with a quantity from 10 l per second to 100 l per second - from BGN 1,000 to BGN 10,000;

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 161 of 236

d) (amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) with a quantity over 100 l per second - from BGN 10,000 to BGN 25,000;
2. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) uses water bodies, water management facilities and systems or constructs such without the necessary grounds for this or in deviation from the conditions provided for in the permit - from BGN 2,000 to BGN 10,000;
3. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) pollutes waters, destroys the beds or banks of rivers in violation of the prohibitions contained in Art. 132, 134, 143 and 144 - from BGN 5,000 to BGN 15,000;
4. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) violates the rules for declaring, reporting and controlling during the implementation of the permitted water abstraction or use of a water body - from BGN 150 to BGN 1,000;
5. damages water management and hydrometric facilities and devices or violates the proper operation and the regulated regimes of their work - from BGN 500 to BGN 5,000;
6. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) discharges wastewater into water bodies and the sewerage system, violating the emission norms and requirements - from BGN 1,000 to BGN 5,000;
7. uses the lands appurtenant to the water bodies or the lands of the coastal floodplains for purposes other than their intended use - from BGN 2,000 to BGN 10,000;

9. conceals project documentation for sites that may affect the natural state of the waters - from BGN 5,000 to BGN 10,000;

11. destroys or falsifies data and information - from BGN 1,000 to BGN 10,000;
12. (amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) fails to fulfill the obligation to notify the competent authorities of circumstances relevant to the protection of waters and protection from their harmful effects - from BGN 200 to BGN 2,000;

13a. (new - SG, No. 55 of 2018) damages or destroys elements of the control and measuring systems of dams - from BGN 10,000 to BGN 25,000;

(2) The natural person or the representative of the legal entity who ordered or allowed the commission of the acts under para. 1 is also punished with the penalty under para. 1, when the acts themselves constitute an administrative violation.
(3) When the violation under para. 1, items 2, 3, 7 and 13 is the carrying out of construction, the fine or sanction is from BGN 10,000 to BGN 25,000.
(4) For a repeated violation under paras. 1 and 2, the fine or sanction is from BGN 1,000 to BGN 50,000.

**Art. 200a.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) (1) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 61 of 2010) An official who allows the connection of new consumers discharging wastewater to the sewerage systems of populated areas, settlement and resort formations, in cases where the sewerage system cannot ensure the discharge and treatment of

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

---
Page 164 of 236

wastewater before amending the issued or issuing new permits for the discharge of wastewater and before the construction or expansion of the necessary facilities for wastewater treatment, shall be punished with a fine from BGN 5,000 to BGN 15,000.
(2) An official who does not fulfill his duties under the law or allows another person not to fulfill his duties under the law, outside the cases under para. 1, shall be punished with a fine from BGN 500 to BGN 1,000.
(3) An official who violates imperative provisions of the normative acts for the implementation of this law shall be punished with a fine from BGN 500 to BGN 1,000.

**Art. 200b.** (New - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, rep. - SG, No. 77 of 2012, in force from 09.10.2012)

**Art. 201.** (1) (Amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The acts for establishing the violations under Art. 200, para. 1 with the exception of the violations under items 16 and items 34 - 41 are drawn up by officials authorized by the Minister of Environment and Water or by the directors of the basin directorates.
(2) (Amend. - SG, No. 81 of 2000, amend. and suppl. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, suppl. - SG, No. 58 of 2015) The penal decrees under para. 1 are issued by the Minister of Environment and Water or by officials authorized by him or by the directors of the basin directorates.
(3) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006) The acts for violations under Art. 200, para. 1, items 2, 5 and 7 are also drawn up by officials authorized by the authorities under Art. 190, paras. 1 and 2.
(4) (Suppl. - SG, No. 81 of 2000, amend. - SG, No. 108 of 2001, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 36 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 82 of 2009, in force from 16.10.2009, amend. - SG, No. 93 of 2009, in force from 25.12.2009, amend. - SG, No. 66 of 2013, in force from 26.07.2013, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2014, in force from 28.11.2014, amend. - SG, No. 14 of 2015, amend. - SG, No. 58 of 2017, in force from 18.07.2017) The penal decrees under para. 3 are issued by the Minister of Regional Development and Public Works, the Minister of Agriculture, Food and Forestry, the Minister of Transport, Information Technology and Communications and the Minister of Energy or by officials authorized by the respective minister.
(5) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, rep. - SG, No. 53 of 2014)
(6) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 52 of 2008, amend. - SG, No. 93 of 2009, in force from 25.12.2009, rep. - SG, No. 53 of 2014)
(7) (Amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 70 of 2008

Source: "Ciela" Legal Information Systems 05/11/2021

) The acts for violations under Art. 200, para. 1, items 16 and 34 - 37, as well as under Art. 200, para. 1, items 18 - 20 in cases of exercising control under Art. 155a, para. 3, item 5 are drawn up by officials determined in the Health Act.
(8) (Suppl. - SG, No. 81 of 2000, amend. - SG, No. 65 of 2006, in force from 11.08.2006, amend. - SG, No. 98 of 2010, in force from 01.01.2011) The penal decrees under para. 7 are issued by the director of the regional health inspectorate.
